kumārikākhaṇḍa
nādiphāntākṣarā ye ca pañcāśat pūrvamuddhṛtāḥ 
yathā kuryācca saṃsthānaṃ sṛṣṭinyāye krameṇa tu 
śirohīnamanaṅga tu tathā cākhaṇḍamaṇḍalam 
candrodhvāṅkitameva tu unmanyantaṃ tathā punaḥ 
evaṃ catuḥprakārasthaṃ mālinīnyāsamārabhet 
catuṣṭayavinirmukta nyāsaṃ yaḥ kartumarhati 
nāsau nyāsaṃ na saḥ śiṣyaḥ kṛtaṃ bhavati niṣphalam 
nādabindukalājyotiryeṣu varṇeṣu saṃsthitaḥ 
bījāste sarvata  khyātā  śeṣā varṇāśca kevalā 
kevaleṣu ca varṇeṣu na muktirbhavabandhanāt 
samyakjñāteṣu bījeṣu punarjanma na vidyate 
prākṛtaṃ pūrvakarma tu tailabindurivāmbhasi 
janānāṃ vartamānasya jñātairbīje kṣayo bhavet 
tasmādabhyāsakaraṇa mālinīnyāsarūpataḥ
śaktistu mālinī jñeyā prāṇaśaktiścidātmikā 
suṣumnāntarayogena gamāgamakrameṇa tu 
ravicandrasamāyogāt tadā prasādabhairavam 
prasāda binducakraṃ tu ūdhvaṃ cāṃkuśavartulam 
gambhīranādavegena teṣāṃ sampadyate sukham 
sukhāhlādamanānanda  avasthā prāpyate padam 
tadā sā mālinīśaktirvahnirutpadyate kalā 
sā ca turyasvarākārā vakradehodbhavā kalā 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
candrārkānalakuṇḍeṣu mālinyāyādhikāraṇam' 
viṣavahnigatā madhye āvartante vyavasthitā 
tasmāt sā tiryagā rekhā mālinyākāraveśmani 
tena sā mālinī proktā sthūlā sūkṣmā tathā parā 
parata parayogena parāparaparāyaṇā 
gṛhītvā bījarūpāṇi bindurūpānuyoginī 
tayā vyāptaṃ jagat sarvaṃ aśeṣabhuvanāntikam 
tasyāpyetanmahābīja vāgbhava garbhasaṃyutam 
māyābījaṃ dvitīya tu lakṣmībījaṃ tṛtīyakam 
evaṃ te dīpakaṃ trīṇi bīje bīje pṛthak pṛthak 
śikhāgrādinakhāgrāntaṃ kulavinyāsa sundaram 
dīpakeṣu vinirmukta nyastvā nyāsaṃ ca mālinīm
śiṣyaṃ tatra na mucyeta prākṛtaṃ pūrvakarmaṇā 
pūrvakarmavināśārtha nyāsedida sudīpitam 
kathitaṃ kulayogīnā kaulayogāt paraṃ nahi 
śrīnātha uvāca
caitanyaṃ vyomavigraham 
śiraśchedakanāmena prajvalantaṃ nabhasthitam 
puruṣasyāntarātmānaṃ
sa eva puruṣo vyāpī avyakto jyotirūpakaḥ 
śabdāḍhyaṃ ca guṇātītaṃ prabhutve saṃvyavasthitam 
kiṃ tasya bandhanaṃ proktaṃ raticakre tu bhāvini 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
kimetanmālinīnyāsa mukta bhavati kiṃ prabho 
etad vijñātumicchāmi mālinīkramahetunā 
śrīvakrā uvāca
etat praśnavara guhyaṃ siddhināthāvatāritam 
tasyottara ' pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu ekāgra bhairava 
kṣīramadhye sthitaṃ sarpi avyucchinnaṃ na dṛśyate 
tathāsau puruṣo loke mālinīhadimaṇḍale 
yadā na paśyate jīva svamanena tu sādhakaḥ 
tadāsau vartate karma prākṛtaṃ duratikramam 
sukhaduḥkhavaśaṃ gacchet na jñāta puruṣo yadā 
tadā te pañcabhūtaistu puruṣo'sau vaśaṃgataḥ 
vidite puruṣe deva kṣayasteṣāṃ na saṃśayaḥ 
evaṃ ca prākṛtaṃ karma puruṣasya vyavasthitam 
ādau ca puruṣo vyāpī paścāt karma pravartate 
puruṣeṇa vinā karma na pravarteta bhūtale 
pṛthivyādiṣu tattveṣu saṃsthitaḥ puruṣo hi saḥ 
sattvarajastamaikatve kṛtaṃ karma pravartate 
puruṣeṇa vinā karma na
tasmāccādau ca puruṣaṃ
pravarteta kevalam 
tato bhūtādipañcakam 
paścāt trīṇi guṇānyeṣāṃ
tataḥ karma pravartate 
yasmāt pāśā pravartante śubhāni aśubhāni ca kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
prakṛtyāntargata jñātvā mālinīkuṇḍamadhyataḥ 
pañcabhūtāni mucyeta sādhako mokṣado bhavet 
etat sarva samāsena mālinyā  kramasaṃsthitiḥ 
sā caiva candrarūpeṇa puṃsaḥ śaktiśca cinmayā 
sā ca mātā ca mālinyā sthūlā sūkṣmāparājitā 
bījabhūtā samākhyātā mālinī bhuvanākṛtiḥ 
vaktrād vaktragatā jñeyā guruvako pratiṣṭhitā 
saṃsthitā ceśvare bhāge vāmamārge visarpitā 
tasyāmabhyāsakaraṇa ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ca yathā bhavet 
merumadhyagataṃ vaktraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ  kārayet punaḥ 
dīrgheḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ svarairbhedyai  nādabindulayaṃ kṛtam' 
ṣaḍantaragatā vai ca kuryāt ṣaḍvidhamāsanam 
ṣaḍvadha kāmarājānaṃ mālinyā yoniyojitam 
hṛcchiraśca śikhā varmalocanāstra ca ṣaḍvidham 
devatāṣaḍbhiḥ saṃyukta mālinyāṅgakrameṇa tu 
śavarī vidyujjihvā ca śarvarī ca kulāmbikā 
mohanī māraṇī ṣaṣṭhī pṛthagaṅgeṣu devatāḥ 
kuryād bījatrayaṃ cādau tathā kāmeśvara punaḥ 
devatāmāśramaṃ  ṣaḍbhiḥ ādyanteṣu vilomataḥ 
pṛthakkūṭavidhānena aṅgānyetāni mālinī 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
sakṛdāvartayed yastu satataṃ nyasate'pi vā 
ājñā pravartate tīvrā divyāveśaḥ pravartate 
na śṛṇoti na paśyeta tadāsau muktibhājana 
maṇḍalāgre gurorājñā suvinītaḥ prasannadhī 
vaktrāṇi saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
cchāyācchatraṃ mahādeva ukāra śirasāhatam 
bindvindunāṅkita deva ūdhvavaktraṃ tu mālinī 
haṃsa ca mūrdhni vinyasya vāyubījaṃ ca pūrvataḥ 
ekapādayutaṃ kṛtvā agninā dīptatattvataḥ 
bindvinduśirasākrānta tṛtīyaṃ vaktramaṇḍalam 
agnidhāma ca saṃgṛhya pañcamena samanvitam 
binducandrayutaṃ deva dakṣiṇe vaktramaṇḍale 
vāruṇaṃ māyayā sārdhaṃ dīpanyāyā adhoyutam 
binducandrayutaṃ deva vāmavaktraṃ tu mālinī 
tu
pūtanā dīpanīyuktā mohanyādhaḥ kṛtālayā 
bindu  indusamākrāntā paścime vaktrasaṃsthitāḥ
ete vaktrā mahādeva mālinyāyā prakāśitāḥ 
nyāsedamārabhet śreṣṭha sadyaḥ pratyayakārakam 
asaṃkhyāni ca pāpāni ye kṛtā pūrvajanmani 
ihaloke ca ye cānye kṛtā vātha kariṣyati 
te ca sarve vinaśyanti mālinīnyāsayogataḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
etaccātirahasyaṃ vai merumārgavinirgatam 
śaśicāravaśācchambho ekacakre  adhiṣṭhitam 
tasya yogaprayogo'ya gurorājñāvadhiṣṭhitam 
jānātya yadā deva mālinīkramarājakam 
sa muktaḥ sarvabandhebhyo na bhūyo bandhamāpnuyāt 
tāntrikānā tārkikānāṃ paraśiṣye viḍambake 
na dadyānmālinīnyāsaṃ dattaṃ vā maraṇaṃ bhavet 
tāvad bhramati saṃsāre ghorākāre mahārṇave 
yāvanna  prāpyate deva mālinīkramarājakam 
tathā kula kramaṃ nyāsa kā cintā bhavasāgare 
saubhāgya śreyasaṃpatti aṣṭaiśvaryaḥ pravartate 
bhavate nātra saṃdeho rudravat sādhako bhavet 
etad 
vai mālinīnyāsa sadbhāva kaulikānvaye 
tavākhyataṃ tu siddhasya nādiphāntasvarūpakam' 
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye
kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatisahasra
saṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣite mālinīnyāsakramā
dhikāravarṇane kramodayo nāmānandaḥ  
ūnaviṃśānandaḥ
śrīvakrā uvāca
artha cānyakramaṃ vakṣye śabdarāśisvarūpataḥ 
amṛtādivisargāntaṃ kramaṃ pañcāśadrūpiṇam' 
suśuddhe bhūpradeśe tu pāṃśugomayalepite 
puṣpaprakarasaṃkīrṇe sugupte paśuvarjite 
gurorājñāprasādena śabdarāśi samuddharet' 
yo'sau sarvagato devo vibhuḥ katī sureśvaraḥ 
sa cāmṛtataraṅgeṣu turyastha bindumaṇḍale 
akhaṇḍamaṇḍalākāraṃ yoginīravabheditam 
taṃ para vyomni cakrasya tasya śabdamadhiṣṭhitam 
śabdarāśikrameṇoktaṃ varṇarūpādhikārakam 
piṇḍasthaṃ ca padasthaṃ ca rūpasthaṃ rūpavarjitam 
nirañjanapadāvastha  tadā muktaṃ maheśvara 
śabdabrahma bhavet piṇḍaṃ padaṃ bījākṣaraṃ smṛtam 
rūpaṃ ca maṇḍalaṃ yoga rūpātītaṃ ca bhairava 
nirañjana piṇḍasthaṃ ca rūpasthaṃ rūpavarjitam 
nirañjanapade jñeyāstadādho praśasyate kumārikākhaṇḍa
gurorgurutarāñcaiva ye cānye kramadhārakāḥ 
sarve nirañjanāvasthāstadā te mokṣadāyakāḥ 
śabdabrahma para brahma brahmākṣarasamudbhavaḥ 
tallayaṃ tatparātmānanaṃ brahmavṛkṣaṃ ca golakam 
tasya śākhākṣarā deva pañcāśadrūpasaṃkhyayā 
mantrarūpāstu te sarve pañcāśattanumaṇḍitāḥ 
vyāptisteṣāṃ kramācāra ādhāracandrapuryake 
candrapuryasya vinyasya śabdarāśyādhikārakam 
ānanda tu navātmāna tadā rudrānvaya bhavet 
rudrāṇāṃ mātṛkānyāsaṃ khecarakramanirṇayam 
khecara ca khamadhyasthaṃ madhyasthaṃ ca khakhecaram 
etaccatuḥ prakāreṇa śāmbhavaṃ śabdarāśikam 
anukrama merumārge mudrātattvavibheditam 
tanmadhye ca kramaṃ deva tvaṃ rudra śabdarāśikam 
tvaṃ ca pañcāśadbhirbhedaiḥ prakṛtirjñeyarūpataḥ 
vijñānabhūmikāyoga kārikākramasantatiḥ 
santānamekamākāśa bhedāste saptaviṃśatiḥ 
teṣāṃ mūrtidharaṃ devaṃ varṇarāśyā tu kevalam kumārikākhaṇḍa
śrīnātha devatairyukta sa ca ulitraye guruḥ 
ulitraye kramāḥ trīṇi teṣāṃ rāśiprayojanam 
pūrvokta sahitāyāṃ tu ādināthena svāminā 
tasya mantrakramameva pratyaya pūrvabhāṣitam 
bhāṣāmudrāsamopetaṃ bhairavaṃ śabdarāśikam 
tacca ca tṛtīyakaṃ mārga ādyapīṭhaṃ surendrarāṭ 
asyoddhāra punarhayeva yathā sṛṣṭikrameṇa tu 
ātmānaṃ rudravat jñātvā rudramātmānavad dhara 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ jñātvā śabdarāśyāvatārayet 
amṛtādihakārāntaṃ etad varṇaparam 
mātṛkākulamekaṃ tu bhagajāta tu pratyayam 
tacca pañcāśaddhirbhedaiḥ nyastvā kṣobho'bhijāyate 
etadakṣaravinyāsa pūrvasaṃskārasaṃskṛtam 
tadā bījakramanyāsa avijñāta na mucyate  
anaṅgasya śiraṃ nyasya lalāṭaṃ tava mūrdhani 
tathā caiva ñavarṇasya bhavet tad vaktramaṇḍalam 
tathā prānta  va tejasya ṣoḍhaṃ nyasya tathaiva ca 
tu
dvāvetau nayanau deva candrādityāvabhāsakau 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tathā caiva kalā proktā mahendrasya tu mastakam 
etat karṇadvaya deva savyāsavyau udāhṛtau 
dve kalānte vilomena nāsādvārayutāvubhau 
mahendrādya dvayaṃ pātyaṃ mukhagaṇḍasthalāvubhau 
rāvaṇāntau vilomena adhove dantapaṃktiṣu 
rājendrādyaṃ dvayaṃ ceṣṭau adha ūdhve subhāvite 
girijāsanamuddhṛtya brahmarandhre maheśvara 
tasyādyaṃ yad visargākhyaṃ jihvāmūla vidhīyate 
akārādivisargāntaṃ svaracakramiti smṛtam 
brahmāṇī devatā tatra saṃsthitā śambhumaṇḍale 
athāṅgāni vadedānīṃ śṛṇu tathyaṃ svarūpataḥ 
dvijāsana prabhu pātya tena skandhaṃ tu dakṣiṇam 
siṃhasya āsanaṃ bāhu āsanādyaṃ ca kūrparam 
hanumanta śira pātyaṃ dakṣahasta tadopari 
siṃhāntaṃ ghāntara tasmād dakṣahastanakhāgragam 
kavarga pañcadhā deva māheśvarya samāyutam 
śaktipurasya bimbasya yadādya skandhamuttamam 
tathā tasya śira pātyaṃ vāmabāhuniyojitam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
bhaśira kūrpara caiva ā ādyaṃ karapṛṣṭhagam
māyādyaṃ ca karāṃgulyo  nakhāgreṣu ca vinyaset 
cavarga caiva kaumārya tava deva prakāśitam 
gauryāyā ādimaṃ kārya dakṣiṇe ca sthira kuru 
tasyāsana dakṣata rudra adho jānujaṅghayoḥ 
ḍakārādya gata pādaṃ dakṣiṇetalapṛṣṭhagam 
tadgrahaṃ cāṃgulīyojya  nakhāstathā vai kaulika 
ṭavarga vaiṣṇavīsāra dakṣamārge virājate 
pṛthivyādhaḥ sphijavāma nīrādhaścoruka bhavet 
mahāśaṅkhāsanaṃ jānu jaṃghāyā ca gata smṛtam 
tathā dhūmradhvajasyādhaḥ pādapṛṣṭhamadha  smṛtam 
anaṅgaśiramāśritya pādāṃgulyo nakhāgrataḥ 
vārāhyādhiṣṭhita  varga vinyaset kramapaddhatau 
evaṃ varṇodaye pā pārravadakṣiṇakukṣigam 
nacāntaragataḥ kukṣau tadanye sarvatomukhaḥ 
ṣaśira pṛṣṭivaṃśe tu sṛgūdhvamudara viduḥ 
tadagatānta  mahādeva hṛdaya śabdarāśikam 
indrāṇyadhiṣṭhita varga hṛdayaṃ kulayoginīṃ 
tvaca kapālamūdhvastha śoṇitaṃ jaṭāhārādi 
anantaragata māṃsa anaṅgādhaḥ sthitaṃ snāyu 
catvāro vyāpakāstattvā āgneyā ravimaṇḍale 
viddhi tattvaṃ yavargeda svapiṇḍakalayojitam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tathā majjā phakārāntā harādhaḥ śukramaṇḍalam  
evaṃ śiraṃ kuverasya taccāsthiviniyojitam
madhyasthaṃ madhya  prāṇa pāyutattvamadhomukham 
cāmuṇḍādhiṣṭhita vargaṃ aṣṭamaṃ parisaṃkhyayā 
vargātītamadhaḥsthaṃ tu visargasahitātmakam 
pratimāyā gataṃ deva kopasthānagataṃ viduḥ 
tasya sā navamī devyā mahālakṣmyadhikāriṇī 
amṛtādihakārānta para varṇaparigraham 
mātṛkākramameva tu bhagajāta tu pratyayam' 
evaṃ pañcāśadbhirbhedairādikṣāntaṃ krameṇa tu 
etadakṣaravinyāsa pūrvasaṃskārasaṃskṛtam 
varṇabījakramanyāsa avijñāta na muñcati 
śabdabrahmākṣarā yānti saṃskārakṛtaraśmayaḥ
kṛtakṛtyakramādyaugha prākṛta tu surādhipa 
śabdavarṇākṣarāṇāṃ tu sṛṣṭirādyā kramodaya 
anulomena siddhasya tena tvaṃ śabdarāśikam 
śabda tu pṛthivyantastha pṛthivyāṃ hara mālinī 
mālinyā śabdarāśyā tu otaprota jagatrayam 
kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
dīpanena vinirmukta antaḥśūnya maheśvara 
tasmāt tacchabdarāśyādau dīpanaṃ samudāharet 
yānujaṃ kharamadhyasthaṃ gajendrabhujabheditam 
candrakāntiśikhābhinnaṃ hṛdayaṃ kulakhecarī 
bīje bīje pṛthak deva kṛtvādau vīravigraham 
sudīptaṃ bhavate nyāsaṃ mālinīpraṇavatraye 
ādyante saṃpuṭa kṛtvā śabdarāśyāmanena tu 
tathā saṃpuṭitaṃ nyāsaṃ nyaset vaktrāṅgasaṃyutam 
vṛṣabhaṃ madhyagaṃ gṛhya śaktyāsanavyavasthitam 
saṃvarta ca mahākālaṃ pinākī tadadhasthitam 
etat kūṭaṃ samākhyātaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ kārayet punaḥ 
hrasvaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ svarairbhedya indubinduralaṃkṛtam
ūdhvamūdhve tathā pūrve paścime dakṣiṇottare 
vaktranyāsa mahādeva pūrvabījaiḥ pradīpitam 
tūṣṇīśaṃ ca kulīśa ca śrīkaṇṭhāghorabhairavam 
uttareśa anantīśaṃ paścimena sadāśivam 
b
ete siddhā niyuktavyā vaktraṣaṭke varānana 
athāṅgāni pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepeṇa vadāmyaham 
vṛṣabhaṃ madhyamaṃ sthāpya harasyāsanabheditam 
atādiṣu sutaṃ kuryāt hṛcchireṇa vibheditam 
nīlakaṇṭhaśiraṃ kṛtvā kūṭeda ṣaḍvidhoddharet 
dīrdhaiḥ ṣaḍbhi' svarairbhinna kalābinduśivāṅkitam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
aghoraṃ hṛdi saṃyukta amoghaṃ śirabhūṣaṇam 
nīlakaṇṭha śikhā' yojya varmasthamekavīrakam 
piṅgalaṃ netraryonyasya kapilās ca bhairavam 
evaṃ tu bhairavai  ṣaḍbhiryuktā aṅgāni vinyaset 
dīpanādya tataḥ kṛtvā bhavennyāsa tu saṃpuṭam 
saṃpuṭena tu riktāṅgā antaḥśūnyā gabhastayaḥ 
vyāpakatvena tiṣṭhanti sudīptā vyāpakāstu te 
eṣo vai śabdarāśistu sudīptāṅgasamāyutaḥ 
kramasyāgre nyased yastu brahmahā api śuddhyati 
satataṃ nyasate yastu jīvanmuktyariho bhavet 
nirāmayo bhaved vidvān kṛtaiḥ pāpairna lipyate 
siddhatulyo bhavet so'pi śabdarāśiprabhāvataḥ 
ājñākṣobhastathā ghūrmi āveśa ca muhurmuhuḥ 
bhavate parasavittiryatra sā ramate parā 
parasthānapadaprāptirmukto bhavati bandhanāt 
etad vai śabdapuruṣa brahmaśabdairadhiṣṭhitam 
adhiṣṭhāna tu kaulasya pratyaya śabdarāśikam 
rāśau pañcāśadbhedāni śabdaka vāgbhavoditam 
śabdarāśiḥ smṛtastena rudratvamūrtibhairava 
tasya mūrtirnavātmāna śāsane kuladīpakam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tasyoddhāraṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvekāgra sundara
bhṛgulākulasaṃvarto mahākāla pinākinam' 
khaḍgīśaṃ ca bhujaṅgākhyaṃ vālīśaṃ cārghanāyakam 
kalābindvaṅkitaṃ nāda jyotirūpa caturthakam 
eṣu deva navātmāna vṛkṣīśaṃ vṛkṣanāyakam 
mūrtibhūtaṃ kalāyāñca paramānandabhairavam 
tasyāśramaṃ brahmavṛkṣaṃ trivalītaramārgagam 
turyāntaṃ maṇḍalaṃ śāktaṃ tatrānandaḥ  pravartate 
tatra saṃbhāvayet piṇḍaṃ dīpanaṃ śabdarāśikam  
himakundendudhavalaṃ śatārkavapuṣojjvalam 
tasyotsaṅgagatā devī ahameva tu mālinī 
taddharmadharmiṇī deva tasya mūrtidharī śubhā 
māyābījena tejāḍhyā arghasthāne niyojitā 
dāḍimodakasaṃkāśā sphuraṇāḍhyā virājate 
aṃkurākārarūpeṇa brahmagranthī hyadhomukhī 
kubjikā pararūpeṇa akārāntā śivāvadhiḥ 
śivaśaktirvilomābhyāṃ viśrāmamaṃ hṛdi maṇḍale 
ūdhve śivamadha śakti prasara  madhyabhūmikā 
tatra cotpadyate'vasthā jñātvāveśaṃ muhurmuhuḥ 
turyastha śabdarāśistu yonisthā mālinī svayam 
guruvaktraṃ tayormadhye ānanda ca adhomukham 
yathākramaṃ mahaugho'yaṃ ākhyātaṃ
śivaśaktyayoḥ
kumārikākhaṇḍa
mūrtinyāsa pravakṣyāmi yathā vihito'nukramāt 
brahmarandhre lalāṭe ca vaktre hṛdayamaṇḍale 
nābhau guhye ca urubhyāṃ jaṅghayoḥ pādayugmake 
evaṃ nyāsa samākhyātaṃ pañcaratnairadhiṣṭhitam 
tathā hyaṅgavidhīdānīṃ yathā  vakṣyāmi tacchṛṇu 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśā hṛdi devyā virājate 
śira mañjiṣṭhasadṛśaṃ
śikhā hyulkāgnivad bhavet 
ārakta śuddhadhavala netrau raktau tathobhayoḥ 
astraṃ cāghorasadṛśa śuddhākāśaṃ yathā viduḥ 
etad varṇavibhāga tu jñātvā siddhyariho bhavet 
mālinī śabdarāśistu rudrayoginibṛṃhitam 
dīpanaistu samāyuktaṃ ṣaḍaṅgakramabheditam 
sthānalakṣasamāyuktaṃ dhyānadhāraṇasaṃyutam 
umāmaheśvaraṃ cakraṃ tavākhyātaṃ varānana 
jātibhedavihīnāṅgā jñātavyāḥ pūrvavat kramāt 
kulakaulakramādhāraṃ mālinī śabdarāśikam 
kathitaṃ kulasiddhānta jñeyaṃ mārga maheśvara 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
ityājñāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatāre vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye
kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasahitāyāṃ
avvākramabhāṣite śabdarāśyādhikāravarṇane 
kramodayo nāmānandaḥ 
śrīnātha uvāca
viṃśānandaḥ
mālinī śabdarāśiśca ubhāvetau śrutau mayā 
adhunā' śrotumicchāmi' trividyāṃ kaulinīṃ' parām 
śrīvakrā uvāca
śabdarāśiprasiddhasya punaranyavikalpakam 
idānīmākarṇaya śambho vidyātritayakaulikam 
parā ca aparā caiva tathā caiva parāparā 
teṣāmuddhāraṃ anya tu kathayiṣyāmi suvrata 
prathamā parāparā pañcacatvāriṃśākṣarā' bhavet 
ādyāmṛta ca khaśira gajendrādyavibhūṣitam  
tadgrahasya śiraṃ pātyaṃ tadgrahāsanabheditam 
padmayoniśira gṛhya pārthivāntasamanvitam 
kapālāntakṛta  bindu ardhacandrakṛtānvitam 
padamekaṃ tu prathamaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca yathā bhavet 
tārādyaṃ ca ṭhakārādya tathā cānaṅgamastakam 
pādrai  caikaśire bhadra' tadgrahasyādhimastakam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
madhyamaṃ ca ananṅgaṃ ca agnidhāmavibheditam 
khaśiraṃ khaśirākrāntaṃ kapālāsanamaṇḍalam 
ra eva vedhakākrāntaṃ varṇādyasya tu mastakam 
ekapādasthitaṃ śambho tathā vai merumadhyagam 
kāntayukta maheśāna tṛtīya padamuddhṛtam 
napūrvādyantādha saṃstha yaḍhānta bhānuditam 
haśiraṃ paṅkajasthaṃ tu ghādhaḥstha māyayā yutam 
caturthapadamākhyātaṃ pañcamaṃ cādhunā bhavet 
mādyaṃ gaurīsamāyukta tathā caiva bhānāntagam 
jāsanaṃ īśvarākrāntaṃ rāvāntaṃ rādhagaṃ ca i 
vādyaṃ caivaikavīraṃ tu dvirabhyāsena ṣaṣṭhamam 
ghanāntaṃ māyayā sārdhaṃ anaṅgāsanamaṇḍalam 
dvāvetau ca dvirabhyāsāt padameva tu saptamam 
sayāntaṃ ca dvidhābhūta ekāreṇa dvitīyakam 
aṣṭamaṃ padamevaṃ tu ṭhaantaṃ paṅkajasthitam kumārikākhaṇḍa
vargātītaṃ tu sabhinnaṃ dvidhābhūtaṃ niyojayet 
navamaṃ padamākhyātaṃ visargasthāgnidhāmakam 
kevalaṃ tu dvirabhyāsa daśamaṃ padamuddhṛtam 
viccekādaśameva tu padakramakrameṇa tu 
vāgbhava māyayā sārdhaṃ tathā prasādabhairavam 
ādyamante kṛtaṃ deva uddhṛtā ca parāparā 
pracatvāriṃśatī proktā tasyāmāsanapakṣakam 
vidyā parāparā hyeṣā ādhārāt tu vinirgatā 
eṣāsanaṃ kramasyokta āsanaṃ na mṛgājinam 
vidyārūḍhaṃ kṛtātmāna aparāṃ ca samabhyaset 
māyāpiṇḍaṃ sapheraṃ tu rāvasyodhvamadhaḥ kṛtam 
evaṃ trirakṣarā vidyā ādimena tu yojitā 
ādimaṃ tu yadā cānte tadā sārdhaṃ pada bhavet 
adhyuṣṭā jvalikā devī vidyā aparabhairavī 
eṣā vai mūrtipakṣasya anāhatavinirgatā 
tasyodhva paramaṃ śambho pakṣaṃ tu jagataḥ pṛthuḥ
tava caikākṣarā vidyā sā ca pañcaprakārataḥ kumārikākhaṇḍa
merukarṇikayā jvālā śaṅkhamastakabheditā 
kuverāsanamūdhve tu visargāntamiti smṛtam 
eṣā sā bhagavatī devī nāmnā sā vahnivāsinī 
ekākārā parā mātā viśvamātā pratiṣṭhitā 
śambhumārge sthitā vidyā śāmbhavīsṛṣṭirūpataḥ 
tadadhaḥsthāsana mārga sūkṣmaṃ hṛdayavallabham 
tasyāsana paraṃ nātha tat śāktamiti kaulikam 
śāktaśāmbhavayormadhye āṇava nāma pakṣakam 
a
etat trikaṇṭaka mūlaṃ nyastvā kṣobho vijāyate 
mālinyā śabdarāśestu etad vidyākramatrayam 
abdaikena tu abhyāsāt parāvasthā pravartate 
ye yoginīkule jātā teṣā tuṣṭā hyahaṃ purā 
te jñāsyanti trike bhedān śabdarāśisamāyutān  
pañcāśadrudraracita sthānavarṇaparigraham 
etad deva paraṃ guhyaṃ nyāsaṃ tridaśapūjitam 
trīṇi vidyāstrisiddhāśca tripīṭha ca tridevatam 
trīṇi vṛkṣā guhāstrīṇi  triśaktirguṇamujjvalā 
trināḍimārgagaṃ jñātvā vidyātritayamāruhet 
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare
svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ devyākramabhāṣite
trividyādhikāro nāmānandaḥ ekaviṃśānandaḥ
śrīvakrā uvāca
athānya pravakṣyāmi aghorāṣṭakamuttamam 
gamāgamena kartavyaṃ śivena tu puṭīkṛtam 
padabhedakrama śambho idānīṃ kathayāmyaham 
aghoreti' padaṃ pūrvaṃ aghoyīī dvitīyakam 
eṣā sā prathamā ghorā dvitīyā ca yathā bhavet 
paramaghoreti padaṃ paramaghoyīī' param 
ghorarūpe havisarga ghorarūpā ī cāntagam' 
tṛtīyāghorikā proktā caturthī tvathavā śṛṇu 
ghoramukhi ghoramukhā īkārasvarabheditam 
bhīmabhīṣaṇīti pada aparaṃ bhīmabhīṣaṇā 
gauryā caturthikā gauryā pañcamā ca maheśvara 
vama piva heti padaṃ vama piva hāyīsaṃyutaṃ 
ṣaṣṭhīyaṃ kathitāghorā aparā saptamā bhavet 
ruruśabda raraścaiva ruruśabda raraḥ punaḥ 
akārasthāstvime rephā gauryāyākṣaradīpitāḥ 
eṣā sā saptamā ghoyī aṣṭamā cādhunā bhavet 
phetkārī caiva phetkārya caturthasvarabheditā 
aghoryaṣṭakametad hi padaṣoḍaśabhedataḥ 
dvipadakramayogena kathitaṃ ghorikāṣṭakam kumārikākhaṇḍa
dīpanaistu vinirmukta aghoryādyaṣṭakoddhṛtam 
na tu siddhiprada deva bījahīnaṃ na sādhayet 
tasmāt sabījakaraṇa idānīṃ śṛṇu bhairava 
mātṛkākramaliṅgasya pūrṇimānalabheditam 
gauryāyāmalamākrāntaṃ ājñāvartisamujjvalam 
etad bījaṃ mahendrasya tathā prasādabhairavam 
tasyānte madhyagaṃ pātyaṃ mahendraśirabheditam 
śaktitomaramāviṣṭaṃ adhikārārṇabheditam 
tatpadastha visargasthaṃ vyomabījaṃ maheśvara 
bavilomāccaturtha tu toraṇaśirabheditam 
tasyādhasthastathā codhvaṃ candrāsana susasthitam 
tasyodhve tu punaḥ kṣobha saṃyogād rāvabījakam 
vakārasya makārasya antasthaṃ ca samuddharet 
kuberāsanamāviṣṭa bindubhinnagurūpari 
eṣaiva kaulinībījaṃ surasiddhanamaskṛtam  
prathamādi caturthaṃ tu agnivedhakabheditam 
śaśāṅkāṃkitabindūdhve ṣaṭyāgāt saptame hitam 
eṣa kālāgnirudrastu proktaḥ sarvajanapriyaḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
bhalamadhyamaka nātha bādyenāhata auśiram 
bindunādakalākrāntaṃ mahārudrapuroddhṛtam 
anya dhūmradhvajasyādyaṃ toraṇāsanabheditam 
toraṇa śiracandrā ānanda ca akhaṇḍitam 
yoginībījarājāna rāvāvasthottamottamam 
etad bījāṣṭakaṃ kuryād ghoryāyā aṣṭakasyatu 
padānāṃ ṣoḍaśānāṃ tu bījānyaṣṭau dvidhā kuru 
avasāne padānāṃ tu te bījā ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ 
bhaviṣyanti ca deveśa ādyantaśivayojitāḥ 
prasādasya tu jīvasya śiraṃ kṛtvā caturdaśam 
bhavate śivarājāna kṛtvā nyāsa samārabhet 
padābhyā jānujaṅghābhyāṃ ādhāre hṛdi maṇḍale 
kukṣibhyāṃ pṛṣṭhavaṃśe ca tathā bāhudvaye punaḥ 
vaktramaṇḍalamevaṃ tu aṣṭasthāneṣu vinyaset 
saṃhāra pūrvataḥ kṛtvā tataḥ sṛṣṭikramaṃ punaḥ  
aghoyadyātmaka nyāsaṃ trikaṇṭāvaraṇoddhṛtam 
kathitaṃ tava deveśa puryaṣṭakasamāyutam 
śabda sparśaca rūpa ca raso gandhaśca pañcamaḥ 
a
mano buddhirahaṃkāra puryaṣṭakamiti smṛtam 
brahmāṇyādevatādyaṣṭau catuḥṣaṣṭistu saṃkhyayā 
evaṃ vyāptikrameṇaiva aghoryaṣṭaka vinyaset 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
atha vidyākramaṃ nyāsaṃ siddhagāṅgasamāyutam 
karanyāsakrameṇaiva pūrva yat khyāpitaṃ mayā 
sāmprataṃ bījavinyāsa tathā vai pīṭhapañcakam 
visargādyaṃ mahāvarṇaṃ pañcadhā kārayet svaram 
mahadbhūtamataḥ  kṛtvā dīrghapaṅkajabheditam 
kalābindvaṅkitaṃ deva etad vai bījapañcakam  
vinyastavyaṃ hi devyāyāstattvapañcakasaṃyutam 
pṛthivī śaktibījaṃ tu āpo vai somabījakam 
tejo vai sūryabījaṃ tu vāyurve bindubījakam 
ākāśaṃ nādabīja tu etad vai bījapañcakam 
teṣāṃ sthānāni vai pañca guruvaktre pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
pṛthivī kandacakre tu āpo vai yonimaṇḍale 
tejo vai nābhicakrasthaṃ vāyurhṛdayamaṇḍale 
ākāśaṃ ca bhruvormadhye bījasthānāni pañca ca 
bījabījāśramāḥ pañca kṛtvā ādyena saṃyutam 
labdhvā gurūpadeśaṃ tu nyastavyaṃ bījapañcakam 
anyathā na bhave'vasthā bījahīnā ca sundara 
pṛthivyādiṣu tattveṣu bandha cāstamana bhavet 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
sadābhyāsena kaule'smin punarjanma kuto bhavet 
etadunmanīkaraṇa nyāseda bījapañcakam 
tattvānāṃ pañcakaṃ deva adhikārakrame sthitam 
upadeśe bhavedeva nyāseda pīṭhapañcakam 
uktā ye pūrvaṃ te pañca praṇavāni samabhyaset 
teṣāmagre tu pīṭhāni kṛtvā nyāsa samārabhet 
uttaraṃ pūrvapīṭhaṃ tu pañcamādyantabhūṣitam 
bhrūmadhye kṛṣṇavaṇabhaṃ tathā jālandharaṃ punaḥ 
dvitīyādyantarūpaṃ tu ārakta hṛdi maṇḍale 
tathā pūrṇagirinama tṛtīyādyantaropitam 
pītavarṇaṃ ca nābhistha kāmarūpa tathāparam 
prathamādyantamadhyastha himakundenduguhyataḥ 
tisrove pañcamaṃ pīṭhaṃ caturthādyantayojitam 
haritaṃ tanmahāraudraṃ kandasthāne prakāśitam 
udaya kāmarūpetu sthiti pūrṇagirya 
saṃhāra dakṣiṇe pīṭhe nirvāṇaṃ pañcame sthitam 
viśrāmamādyapīṭhe tu nyāsedaṃ pīṭhapañcakam 
yathā dhyānaṃ tu pīṭhānāṃ kāmarūpādi bhairava 
tathā krameṇa tattvānāṃ kuryād vai dhyānapañcakam 
yathā tattvāni bījāni tathā vai pīṭhapañcakam

sabāhyābhyantaraṃ jñātvā ko na muñcati bandhanāt

tatra sā kaulinī vidyā antaḥkaraṇabheditā

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi nyāsaṃ tridaśapūjitam 
ṣoḍhā dvādaśabhedena nyāsaṃ kuryād gamāgame 
ṣoḍhā śakti samākhyātā parā ekākṣarā śubhā 
tasyāsana ṣoḍhāsaṃjñā ṣoḍhāśaktipuraṃ viśet 
tasya te ṣoḍaśo' bhedā ' śṛṇu mārgeṇa sundara 
jaṭāhāra gauryā sthāpya dvādaśadhā punaḥ 
bindunā bhedita kṛtvā candrārkaśirasāhatam 
tasyāṅgā dvādaśale khyātācchāyācchatramanukramāt 
siṃhāsanaṃ tu prathama cādyāsana dvitīyakam 
tṛtīyaṃ hyekavīra syāt caturthaṃ haramaṇḍale 
pañcamaṃ śaktibījaṃ tu makārāsana ṣaṣṭhakam 
saptamaṃ jilabhāgasya aṣṭamaṃ haramastakam 
haśiraṃ navamaṃ deva daśama tāraṇaṃ śiraḥ 
rājyamekādaśaṃ ceti dvādaśa tārakaṃ nyaset 
vedhake vedhayet sarvān ekavīreṇa bhūṣitān 
candrajyotikalāśuddhāḥ rudradvādaśabheditāḥ 
punareva hi deveśa gaurya dvādaśabhiḥ punaḥ 
rudraśaktisamāyogāt ṣoḍhānyāsaṃ mamākṛtiḥ 
na tasyā dīpanaṃ kiñcid gauryādvādaśadīpitā 
eṣā vai rudraśaktistu ṣoḍhāśaktirnapuṃsakā  kumārikākhaṇḍa
tasyā dvādaśadhānyāsaṃ ādau sṛṣṭikrameṇa tu

kopasthāne ca netrābhyāṃ karṇanāsāpuṭāvubhau 
kaṇṭhe ca hṛdaye nābhau yonau ādhāramaṇḍale 
ṣoḍhānyāsa krameṇokta gauryākādirgamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
āga sṛṣṭibījādau indubinduvikāsitam 
makārādikrameṇaiva gamāgame padadvayam 
sadā nyastena deveśa maṇḍalāgre kramāgrataḥ 
varṣaikena ca abhyāsāt divyājñā saṃpravartate 
dvādaśābde tu saṃprāpte pāṣāṇānapi vedhayet 
cūrṇayet parvataśṛṃgān mudrāsphoṭānyanekaśaḥ 
kurute vividhāñścaryān ājñāveśaprabhāvataḥ 
yaṃ so'valokayejjantuḥ pāśānāṃ vajrapañjaram

kālāntarād guṇotpattimacirāllabhate dhruvam

ājñā sā ca krame guroradhikāra samārabhet

tathā ca dvādaśa ślokā ulitritayanirṇayam kumārikākhaṇḍa

mantrapādena caikena vidyāpādārdhameva ca 
mudrā caivāṣṭabhāgena gurupādaikasaṃjñaka 
nirvāṇe ca niraṃśe ca tadā siddhi labhennaraḥ

śrīvakrā uvāca'
trayoviṃśānandaḥ
adhunā tadgrahaṃ vakṣye vidyātritayabheditam 
vargāṣṭakavidhānena amūlāt' tu vinirgatam 
a' ana a iti padaṃ pūrva ā tha gho tu' dvitīyakam 
i' ṝ re tṛtīyaṃ syāt ī ṝ hrī caturthakam 
u ḷ pa pañcamaṃ' syāt ū lṛ ra ṣaṣṭha smṛtam 
ṝ ca ma saptamaṃ caiva aṣṭamaṃ ṝ dha gho iti 
lṛ ṇa re navame datta lṛ u hrauṃ daśamaṃ smṛtam 
e ū gho daśamekaṃ ca ai ī ramiti dvādaśam 
o baru trayodaśa au ka peti caturdaśam 
aṃ kha haḥ tripañcamaṃ ca aḥ ga gho iti ṣoḍaśaḥ 
ka gha ra saptadaśa ca khaṅa mu ca daśāṣṭakam 
ga i khi ūnaviṃśañca gha a bhī iti viṃśamam 
ṅa va ma ekaviṃśa ca ca bha bhī dvayaviṃśamam 
cha ya ṣa trayoviṃśaṃ ja ḍha ṇi caturviṃśakam 
jha ḍa va pañcaviṃśañca ña ṭha ma ṣaḍviṃśamam 
ṭa jha va saptaviṃśañca ṭha ña ma cāṣṭaviṃśam 
ḍa aḥ pi ūnatriṃśeti ḍha ṭa va triṃśamaṃ padam 
ṇa ra pi ekatriṃśañca ta ja va dvayatriṃśamam 
thapa heti trayastriṃśam de sa he catustriṃśakam 
dhaharu pañcatriṃśañca na ccha ru ca ṣaṭtriṃśakam 
pa la ra saptatriṃśañca pha ā ra aṣṭatriṃśakam 
ba ṣa vi ūnacāriṃśa bhakṣa cce catvāriṃśatiḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
ma ma aiṃ ekacāriṃśa ya śa hrī dvicatvāriṃśam 
ra a hūṃ tricatvāriṃśa la ta hrīṃ catuścāriṃśam 
va e aiṃ pañcacāriṃśa śa ai hrīṃ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśam 
ṣa o aiṃ saptacāriṃśa sa au kṣaṃ aṣṭacāriṃśam 
ha da hrī ūnapañcāśat pha hasrauṃ śatārdhakam 
pañcāśatpadasaṃyogāt saṃgraheṇa tu tadgraham 
śabdarāśikrameṇaiva nyāsaṃ kuryācca tadgrahe 
bhaved divyatanurmayo asya nyāsasya sevanāt 
ṣaṇmāsāt paṭhite siddhiḥ athavābdena niścayāt 
śastraghātairna bhidyeta acchidra vajrayoginaḥ 
kṛtvādau rāvabījaṃ tu padasyānte tathā punaḥ 
rāvabījapuṭāntastha vidyātritayabhedataḥ 
sudīpta tadgraha tasmād bījarikta parāṃmukham 
paradehād viniṣkrāntaṃ yoginīmukhasaṃcayam 
evaṃ tadgrahakṣetraṃ tu vidhānavadaśeṣataḥ 
evaṃ vai kulasaṃcāra kulācāre pratiṣṭhitam 
yasyedaṃ vaktragaṃ nyāsaṃ so'pi śāntapade sthitaḥ 
pūrvābhyastaṃ na saṃdehoṃ anyāyaṃ na pravartate 
śrīvakrā uvāca
punaranyaṃ pravakṣyāmi nyāsaṃ tu samayakramam
padabhedakrameṇaiva vidyā pīṭheśvarī bhavet 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
cce vi ceti padaṃ pūrvaṃ ṇiki ṇiki ca dvitīyakam 
ccha ra ī ca sacandrārdha ccha ra ā sārdhacandramā 
ubhayostṛtīya regho virabhaiyemasa punaḥ 
gala ū saśaśi kṛtvā caturthapadamuddhṛtam 
kahaśabda dvirabhyāsa saṃyogāt padaṣaṣṭhamam 
sahaśabda dvirabhyāsa devatāṣṭapada smṛtam 
hara au candraśūnyasthaṃ dvidhābhūtaṃ navamaṃ smṛtam 
ṇikako dvipañca ca ṇikako daśaikādhikam 
haśakti  śūnyacandrārdhaṃ kalā rephaṃ ca candramā 
gauryā śūnyaṃ kramādekapiṇḍamevaṃ tu dvādaśam 
menaṇañaṅa padaṃ tu idameva  trayodaśam 
haragaurī śaśi śūnyaṃ harā śūnyaṃ ca maulinī 
caturdaśapadaṃ khyātaṃ khimurāgho a eva ca 
pañcadaśa  samākhyātaṃ rāva reghoa ṣoḍaśam 
reghora saptadaśa syāt re rā rā ca daśāṣṭamam 
kebjiku hasau viṃśeti śrīṃ hrīṃ aiṃ pada viṃśamam 
siṃhakrameṇa vākhyātaṃ aiṃkārādi anukramāt 
udaya sūryamārgeṇa somamārgeṇa rodhanam 
candrasūryakrameṇaiva varṇaiśca catuḥṣaṣṭibhiḥ 
samayākhyā kule kaule ādime nāma yojita 
ādyantena samāyuktā bījayuktā manonmanā 
sā ca pīṭheśvarī māyā samayā kulamālinī kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
sā dīptā bījasaṃyuktā bījariktā  adīpitā 
mahāneṣādhikārī yaḥ sevyamānā sa siddhyati 
bījeścaturdaśai   proktā koṃkaṇā jvalabhūṣitā 
lakṣaikena tū japtena rudraśakti pravartate 
anayā jñātamātrayā sakṛdāvartanādapi 
vidyāyāḥ smaraṇādeva uddhāroddhṛtamātrataḥ 
smaraṇādapi saubhāgyaṃ mahāpāpakṣayo bhavet 
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paṭhanādeva naśyati 
tatkṣaṇānmucyate śiṣyo cakre vā maṇḍalāntare 
vidyāpīṭhopapīṭhe ca yoginīcakramadhyataḥ 
ekavṛkṣe śmaśāne ca melake vā catuṣpathe 
tarpaṇāt pātrasaṃpūrṇe viśvāmitrakapālake 
athavā nṛkapāle ca pūjayet tarpayet tataḥ' 
samayalopād mucyeta tejaścāyu parākramam 
vartate jñānasadbhāva yoginīkulamelakam  
labhate samayāyukto vīradravyaṃ caruṃ tathā 
prāśanād bhavate siddhiḥ anyathā maraṇaṃ bhavet 
nirviśaṅke pade prāpte saṃgrāhyaṃ samayākramam
samayācarukaṃ prāśyaṃ sarvasiddhiphalapradam 
vratastho vratahīno vā asamayī samayī bhavet 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
adīkṣito dīkṣito'sau durbhagaḥ subhago bhavet 
alpāyuṣo dīrghamāyurdaridro dhanavān bhavet 
samayavidyādharo mantrī vīradravyasamāśritaḥ 
tasyādhikāramatula śāstre'smin kaulinīpure 
samayavidyāvinirmukto kulācāravivarjitaḥ 
mantrācāraviluptastu dīkṣito'pi paśurbhavet 
samayabhaṅgeṣu dāridrya maraṇa gurulaṅghanāt 
ājñābhaṅge kutaḥ siddhiracirānnaraka vrajet 
gopayeta kulācāra gurvaugha ca kulāgamam 
naivedyaṃ carudravyaṃ ca yat kiñcit kramasaṃsthitam 
mama vidyāvratasthastu prāśayed samayāgrataḥ 
gurūcchiṣṭaṃ tu caruka samayāyutamantritam
sāṣṭāṅgapraṇipātena kṛtvā maṇḍalaka punaḥ 
hastayorubhayoḥ kṛtvā dehyanujñāṃ prasādataḥ 
evamuktastu śiṣyeṇa guruvaktraprasādataḥ 
prāśanāt kaulikī siddhirnirvikalpasya nānyathā 
nyāsaṃ vidyādhunā vakṣye sṛṣṭinyāyena kaulikam 
ādyārṇasaptaka
repha tṛtīyakaṃ cakṣuṣe kopā ca vinyaset

karṇaubhayordeva kubjike
vaktre rā rā cakṣudvaye smṛtau
kulanāyikā 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
aghore nāsikāgre tu triśūlaṃ vinyasediti 
jihvāyā rāvabījaṃtu aghorā cāsanatraye 
mukhi uṣṭadvayāropya hrāṃ hrīṃ gaṇḍasthalāvubhau
