mekāra
ṇakāra cakrakādyā
hṛdayātmāna
 iti galamekhalā 
hūṃkāra prāṇamadhyataḥ 
koṃkaṇi stanayoretat trikamevānuvinyaset 
koṃkaṇa udare nyasya ikāra nābhimaṇḍale
hrauṃ hrauṃ  karayoḥ kahau hasaśabda tu pṛṣṭhataḥ 
hasaśabdānvitaṃ caiva skandhayoḥ kaha vinyaset 
kahānyaṃ bāhuyugme tu glakāra yonimaṇḍale 
sahaśabda karābhyāṃ tu samayeti karāṃgulī 
bhairavīti tathāghore cchā ccha ūrukayugmake  
kiṇīti jānujaṅghābhyāṃ kiṇi pādadvaye nyaset 
vicce pādāṃgulīprānte vāgbhavaṃ vaktramadhyataḥ 
yatra sthānāt samārabhya kṛtaṃ nyāsaṃ ca vidyayā 
pādāntāt punastatraiva uccāro yatra tallayaḥ 
udayāstamameva tu pu parigīyate 
eṣā sā samayā vidyā apasavyād vinirgatā 
tadgrahasya tu kṣetrasya eṣā evādhikāriṇī 
kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
vidyānyāsena siddhyeta kūṭenaiva vidhānataḥ 
pañcopacārapūjāyāṃ maṇḍalāgre gurogrataḥ
vidyāpīṭhe'thavā cakre yatra kramāgrataḥ
kramāgrataḥ kṛtam 
tatra tasya mahāvasthāpratyaya kaulikaṃ bhavet 
tasya devyāśca kāruṇyaṃ kurute svapnadarśanam 
sarvadvandvavinirmukta acirāt khecaraṃ padam 
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate
śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avākramabhāṣite tadgrahasamayavidyādhikāravarṇanakramo
nāmānandaḥ caturviṃśānanda
śrīnātha uvāca
śrutaṃ vakre 'mayā 'vākyaṃ kumārīkhaṇḍanāyike 
kathaṃ sā mātṛkā nāma ślokadvādaśabheditā'  
na jñātā ca mayā' devi ślokārthaṃ kathaya sphuṭam 
śrīvakrā uvāca
mahānandavikāsena yat tvayā pṛcchitā' hyaham 
tatsarvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi mātṛkākramanirṇayam 
yo'sau parāparo'nantaḥ vibhuḥ kāraṇamavyayaṃ 
praśāntamaparaṃ nāma śāntātītamanāmayam 
pūrvasaṃkṛtyamākāraṃ bhairavasya maheśvara 
kalpe parāmpare pūrvaṃ manvantaraśatairapi 
yugaiścaturaśītiḥ pāṣaṇavat yā tu saṃsthitā 
ekāhaṃ bhairave yajñe bhairava tvamahaṃ punaḥ 
na strī na puruṣākāraṃ nākāraṃ vi kvacit 
śūnyākāre tamaikatve ramaṇānandacetasam 
śamana kulasaṃkāśaṃ kiñcijjānāmyahaṃ hara 
na vācā śruticakṣubhyāṃ na ca buddhyāmyaha hara 
kaivalyānandamāhlāda saṃvatantaṃ śatārdhakam 
tasyecchā kiñciccinmātraṃ avyakta vyaktirūpiṇam 
tadāha  vismayamāpannā kimidaṃ śūnyarūpakam kumārikākhaṇḍa
iti matvā gahana ghoraṃ bhītāhaṃ suptacetasā 
praviṣṭā bhairave yajñe sthitāhaṃ pararūpataḥ 
paramāṇusvarūpeṇa kiñcidrūpaṃ ca siṃhakam 
siṃhasaṃvartaka nātha vyāvṛtaṃ tamasākulam 
akulādikula caiva vyākulaṃ kulakaulikam 
kalanāt dhvaninādāntaṃ tannāda pañcadhāgatam 
tacca ca varṇāditattvaṃ ca kalānāṃ ca mahodayam 
kalāḍhya ca tathā śānta savisargādi cālayam 
mahogra kālika rāvaṃ rūpākhyaṃ ca tathāparam 
kulāvalitayogena vinyaset kulapaddhatim 
dvādaśāni tu ślokāni karṇāt karṇagatāni ca 
sadoccāraprayogena gṛhṇate sādhakottamaḥ 
tasya deyamida  jñānaṃ anyathā na kadācana' 
pañcapraṇavasaṃghātaiḥ sāmānyaireva bhairava 
haṃsākhyairmahatairdivyaiḥ parāmūrtiradhiṣṭitaiḥ 
uddhared dvādaśa ślokān ṣaṭkūṭādhiṣṭhitān śubhān 
catvāraḥ ṣoḍaśairbhedaistathā ṣaṭ nabhāntare 
sṛṣṭimadhyagatā ye ca hakṣasthā dvayabhedataḥ 
kathaṃ yugmaṃ kathākhyaṃ ca anaṅgaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃyutam 
tadadho hanumān nātha rāvamārgasamanvitam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
gajendraśirasākrāntaṃ bindunādakalāṅkitam
ājñājyotisamāyukta ślokadvādaśanirṇaye 
dvitīyamakṣara proktaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu yathā bhavet 
vyomabinduśirobhinna
nādaśaktikalāyuktaṃ mahogramiti kathyate 
amṛtaṃ sravamāṇa ca śāntayuktaṃ samuccaret 
dvirabhyāsa mahāśambho yāvad vai mātṛkākṣaram 
agnivedhakabheditam 
etad vinyāsavijñānaṃ paramaṃ devadurlabham 
kulāvalitayogena uddhāya kulapaddhatiḥ 
sahitārthamida satyaṃ akathyaṃ tava darśitam 
yo'sau parāparo devo bhairavo bhavacchedakaḥ 
tasya icchā hyanāmākhyā kiñciccetā cinoti yat 
sā ca vai vyāpakatvena saṃpūrṇa kaulinī parā 
amā sūkṣmā anāmā ca nirānande layaṃgatā  
sā ca vai bhairavī śāntā anantena vibhājitā 
tasmānmanthānabhedena bheditaṃ ca parāparam 
evaṃ sṛṣṭigatānaṅga anaṅgaṃ kāmanāśanam 
tacca haṃsa mahātmāna jvalanādamṛtodbhavam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
dvāvetau śivaśaktyākhyau otaprota jagatrayam 
etad rahasyamākhyātaṃ mahāmanthānasaṃjñayā 
śrīnātha uvāca
kathaṃ nāthe kā me saṃjñā kutrotpattau nirāmaye 
vyākulo'haṃ samutpanno niḥsaṃdigdha vadasva me 
śrīvakrā uvāca 
sarahasyaṃ kṛtaṃ praśna amoghājñā kuleśvara 
kathayāmi na saṃdeho icchā kāmadugdhāṃ kalām 
yathāhaṃ cidghanānandā ānandatanutāṃ gatā 
tena tṛptiḥ purāsmāka bhavate pṛthivī hara 
pṛthivyāha tva mahacchabda śabdabrahmākṣarāṇi ca 
sā ca śrīśāmbhavecchākhyā suśāntamiti lakṣaṇam' 
ahaṃ kācit kalā kālī vikalā kulaśāmbhavī 
icchā hyahaṃ parotpannā avyaktā vyaktarūpiṇī 
kulālī kulakauleśī akulādvyāpakī bhavet 
vyāpakatvena rūpeṇa saṃyogādupajāyate 
saṃyogena tu saṃvatī nirāvartīt pravartitā 
prathamaṃ ca anāmākhyaṃ nityaṃ ca śiraśekharam 
mahābhairavajyotiśca vyāpakaṃ paścime gṛhe 
eva ṣaṭkakrama tva hi vidyā vyomena veṣṭitā kumārikākhaṇḍa
udaya vimalaṃ nāma amṛta bindubhairavam 
saṃyogena samutpannā tadānte dvādaśa  smṛtāḥ 
mama mūrtigatā kuryāt sṛṣṭihetūpalakṣaṇām 
ahaṃ sā ca parā caikā aparā siddhisāgare
sāgara manmatha nāma kulākulakulāntagam  
trikulaṃ trīṇi tattvāni tridhā mantrī ca śaktayaḥ 
trīṇi siddhāstrayastrotastritattva tripathāntaram 
tatparaṃ ca mahāsthānaṃ mayā vyāptaṃ tu sāgaram 
sāgara śaśisūryantaṃ akhaṇḍamiti maṇḍalam 
akhaṇḍamapara caiva anantaścākṣayaṃ tathā 
akulaṃ pañcamaṃ nātha vijñeyā kulabhūṣaṇā 
evaṃ nādaḥ samutpannaḥ pañcadhā tu kramāgataḥ 
kramāt sṛṣṭi sthitā yonau ekā eva hyadhomukhī 
sadbhāva sā mahāmūrtijyotirūpā manonmanī 
unmanā manavegena śakti kuṇḍalinī kalā 
amā nāma kalā kālī sthitāhatāca bhairava 
asyāścaivāsana pātraṃ iḍānāmena gīyate 
iḍā sā bhairavī śāntā  śaktipātramudāhṛtā 
udaya śaśibimbasya sūryaṃ muñcati bhāsvaram 
tacca bindu ghana ghoraṃ ghargharāmṛtasaṃbhavam 
śāmbhavaṃ ṣaṭkabhedena kalā kalati kaulinī 
maphrekhasaharāveṇa sthitāgniprakṛtirūpiṇī 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
sattvarajatamaikatve sthitā vyomāntavartinī 
vyomyāditattvasaṃghāta  tattvād varṇā hyajāyanta 
ākrāntāśca kalairjñeyā pañcakādisvabhāvataḥ 
pañca bhūtāḥ svarāḥ pañca sūkṣmaśāmbhavasaṃbhavā'
śāmbhava  sarahasyeda rephakhasahakārakam 
tasyaiva vaktramādyaṃ ca anāmānāmasaṃyutam 
yathā sṛṣṭikrameṇokta tathā śṛṇu maheśvara 
vyoma jīvasamāyuktaṃ vahnirardhīśasaṃyutaḥ 
anugrahaśirākrāntaṃ sūkṣmanādena bheditam 
binducandrakalākrānta akṣara bhairava hara 
śūnya khecarasaṃyukta pharamante samāśritam 
ekapādena saṃbhinnaṃ nādabindukalāṅkatam 
eṣā sā khecarīvidyā trailokyākarṣaṇī parā 
yasamadhyagataṃ devaṃ hadhamadhyagataṃ punaḥ 
ṇaṭamadhyagataṃ gṛhya tadantaragataṃ viduḥ 
gaurīśikharamākrāntaṃ indubindukalānvitam 
kathitā śāṅkarī vidyā tṛtīyā kulanāyikā 
caturthī māyayā nāma hara vyomāsanasthitā
agnidhāmena saṃbhinnā i u  madhyagatena ca 
bindu  ardhakalāyuktā raudrarūpā ca ambikā kumārikākhaṇḍa
akathyamātṛkā śakti  hasaphrekārabheditā 
nādabindukalāyuktā vāgbhavākārarūpiṇī 
kaulinī kulanāthānāṃ siddhānāṃ jñānabhūmikā 
śāmbhavāḥ praṇavāḥ pañca ṣaṣṭhaṃ caitanyamuttamam 
ṣaḍaṅgavaktrasaṃyuktā pūrṇā devī parāparā 
ṣaḍbījānukrameṇaiva uccared gurūpadeśata 
dviṣaṭkadivyayogena ślokadvādaśapaddhatim 
yo vetti mahatīṃ śambho ślokārthapadasaṃyutām 
so'pi ekena janmena kaulikājñādharo bhavet 
yaṃ yaṃ spṛśati hastena yaṃ yaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā 
yaṃ yaṃ smarati bhāvena sarva saṃpadyate kṣaṇāt 
duṣṭānyanekakrūrāṇi bhūcaroragarākṣasāḥ 
tasyālokanamātreṇa palāyanti daśo diśaḥ 
iti satyaṃ mayā proktaṃ ślokārthamatamuttamam 
ye nyasyanti trikālajñāste yānti paramāṃ gatim 
śrīvakrā uvāca
atha cānyakramaṃ vakṣye ślokadvādaśake sthitāḥ 
dvādaśa siddhayoginyo abhidhānena tāḥ
śṛṇu 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
nandā bhadrā jayā kālī karālī vikṛtānanā 
kroṣṭukī bhīmabhadrā ca vāyuvegā hayānanā 
gambhīrā ghoṣaṇī caiva yoginyo dvādaśa smṛtāḥ 
kṛtvādau vāgbhavāstrīṇi ante te'pi vilomataḥ 
saṃpuṭena yutā devyo dvādaśāṅgaprasiddhaye
nandā śirasi vinyasyā bhadrākhyā ca lalāṭake 
jayā ca dakṣiṇe netre kālī caiva ta vāmake 
tu
karālī dakṣiṇe karṇe vāme ca vikṛtānanā 
kroṣṭukī  nāsikāgre tu bhīmarudrā tathā mukhe 
vāyuvegā gale caiva hṛdayasthā hayānā 
gambhīrā nābhimadhye tu ghoṣinyā guhyamadhyataḥ 
evaṃ nyāsaṃ tu devīnāṃ divyadehakaraṃ param 
etadāvaraṇaṃ nyāsaṃ dvādaśāṅgamudāhṛtam 
samayasya tu siṃhasya yoginyo dvādaśa smṛtāḥ 
etanyāsa purā kṛtvā yatra yatra vrajennaraḥ 
tatra tatra mahālābhaṃ jñānaṃ labhati puṣkalam 
melakaṃ yoginīsā guptānāṃ ca maheśvara 
dvādaśāṅgaprabhāvena jñānaṃ tāḥ kathayanti hi 
dadanti carukaṃ divyaṃ prasannāstvaritāṃ gatim 
divyarūpadharo yogī yadi gupto maheśvara 
punaranyakrama vakṣye nyāsaṃ kṣetraparigraham 
amṛtādi ca jīvāntaṃ hakṣasaṃjñāsamāyutam 
tāvannyāsa prakartavyaṃ śabdarāśikrameṇa tu 
upadeśa pravakṣyāmi paraṃ devyāḥ parigraham 
dīpanaṃ ca prakartavyaṃ varṇe varṇe pṛthak pṛthak 
hakṣa saṃjñādvayaṃ sthānaṃ prāṇa krodhaṃ ca khe balam
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tābhyāṃ na dīpanaṃ deyaṃ svabhāvenaiva dīpitāḥ 
varṇadīptātmaka piṇḍaṃ ādikādikrameṇa tu 
ādikādikrama kṣetraṃ parādevīparigraham 
dīpamānandayoga ca śakterjñeya parigraham 
ādau vai svaracakraṃ tu tattvaṣoḍaśanirṇayam 
ye ca uktā kakārādyā jīvaṃ te  sarvadehinām 
visargeṇa tu niṣpatti etat kṣetraparigraham  
krodhaḥ prāṇakalā coktā rudraśaktyā ca veṣṭitā 
tābhyāṃ saṃyogakaraṇa guruvaktrāt samabhyaset 
sṛṣṭinyāyena mūrdhādinyāsa kṣetraparigraham 
kṣetraparigrahe hīne matyaiḥ sādhyaṃ na siddhyati 
teṣāṃ tu sādhanāthīya ākhyāta ca parigraham 
anenābhyasite deva ājñāyāmabhiṣecanam 
abhyāsād hi māsaikena pratyaya pravartate 
na śṛṇoti na paśyeta tadā kṣetraparigraham 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi adhikāra punastrayaṃ 
yena vijñātamātreṇa adhikāra  pravartate 
ulīnā tritayaṃ deva jyeṣṭha madhyaṃ kanīyasam 
bālakramaṃ tu kaumāraṃ vṛddhameva kramatrayam 
teṣāṃ kūṭatrayaṃ śambho parādehād vinirgatam kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
prāṇātmādyantanikara ādisthaṃ ca nitambakam 
vāmastanaṃ tathā kaṇṭhaṃ daṇḍaṃ ca skandhadakṣiṇam 
punaḥ prāṇaṃ punardaṇḍa kṣīramekatra piṇḍitam 
evamekādaśā rudrā ekatra viniyojitāḥ 
rudrakūṭaṃ samākhyātaṃ khaṃ candrārdhavibheditam 
dīpitaṃ chinnamuṇḍena etad vṛddhakramoddhṛtam 
tadeva kṣīranirmuktaṃ nāsikayā vibheditam 
kaumārakramakūṭedamākhyātaṃ tava sundara 
taccaiva caiva nāsayā rikta vāmakuṇḍalabheditam 
tṛtīyaṃ ca kaniṣṭhaṃ ca bālakramamudāhṛtam 
olitritayavinyāsa kuryāt kūṭatrayaṃ guruḥ 
jyeṣṭhaṃ ca vinyaseccakre bhrūmadhye kopamaṇḍale ' 
madhyamaṃ nābhideśe tu kaniṣṭhaṃ kāmarūpataḥ 
tribhiraulikrame jātā ye śiṣyā  siddhasantatau 
teṣāṃ tu trividhaṃ nyāsaṃ ākhyātaṃ satataṃ hitam 
krameṇānena deveśa ityājñā pārameśvarī 
tatkṣaṇāt tatra tacchāpa kramaṃ tatra parāṃmukham 
svatulyāṃ guruḍadyaṃ    tu nirbījaṃ pūjayanti ye 
saṃsāre vartate bhūya saṃsārānna nivartate 
na teṣāṃ dīpanaṃ kiñcit śāmbhavakūṭadīpitāḥ 
tasmāt kūṭasthavinyāsa tridhā mantrakramoddhṛtam 
viparyāyakrameṇaiva te ca siddhāstribhiḥ punaḥ 
okāraśca ṣakāraśca mikāraśca triulikāḥ 
nāyakāstatra vinyasya teṣāṃ piṇḍa svarūpataḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
upadeśena vinyāsaṃ karotyāveśamuttamam  
kaniṣṭhaṃ madhyamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ madhyamaṃ yonimadhyataḥ 
aparaṃ yat kaniṣṭhaṃ ca yonimadhye tṛtīyakam 
evaṃ krameṇa vinyāsaṃ na kuryādapi cānyathā 
adhikāratraya śambho jñātvā yajanamārabhet 
ratnapañcakavinyāsa vakṣyāmyāhamataḥ param 
siddhasaṃketasiddhānāṃ prokta sarvatra pañcakam 
tṛtīyaṃ daśanaṃ devyāstasyātmānaṃ hṛdi punaḥ 
nitambaṃ ca śikhā tasyā dakṣastanavibheditam  
vāmakuṇḍalasaṃpūrṇa khaśaktiśivabheditam  
ratnapañcakamākhyātaṃ proktaṃ sarvajanapriyam
oṣamaitracasiddhānāṃ siddhaṃ hyamarikākramam 
lābhya tena ca gūḍhārthaṃ prakaṭaṃ kulakaulikam 
karmakṣayānmahādeva vidyeya pañcadhā bhavet
sevyā santāne satataṃ tataḥ kamariho bhavet  
ratnādyaṃ yat paraṃ piṇḍaṃ tacca ādhāramaṇḍale 
caturthaṃ kaṇṭhadeśe tu pañcamaṃ turyamaṇḍale kumārikākhaṇḍa
b
ekavīrān nyaset pañca na teṣāṃ dīpanaṃ kvacit 
aiṃkārāntarayogena bhagamadhye layaṃgatāḥ 
kṣetrasthā vinyaset pañca svabhāvena ca dīpitāḥ 
cirāyunyāsamātreṇa acchidro bhavate naraḥ 
divyapīṭhapurakṣobhaṃ vīrasiddhimavāpnuyāt 
prāpnoti vividhān bhogān vīraiḥ pañcāśadbhiḥ saha 
yadyāvartayate deva smaraṇāt paṭhanādapi 
sarvasiddhyālayaṃ tasya yoginastu pravartate 
divyadṛṣṭi purakṣobhaṃ siddhiḥ pañcāśritena tu 
daśalakṣakṛte jāpye tīvrājñā saṃpravartate 
pañcaratnena saṃsiddhi nirvāṇaṃ prāpyate padam 
matārthaṃ pūrvato jñātvā mantrapada sphuṭam 
etad vai kaulikaṃ sūtraṃ ṣoḍhānyāsena veṣṭitam  
ṣoḍaśānvayamantraughaṃ kramaṃ ṣoḍaśarūpiṇam 
etad vimalavijñāna  kulamārgavinirgatam 
kulaṃ ca ṣoḍaśairbhedaiḥ santāna ṣoḍaśai punaḥ 
ṣoḍaśājñāprasūtistu nyāsamañjūṣakoddhṛtam 
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena tāntrikānāṃ na darśayet 
evaṃ prabhāvamākhyātaṃ ṣoḍhānyāsasya sundara kumārikākhaṇḍa
gurūpadeśato jñeyaṃ saṃhitārthasamuccayam 
vistaraṃ pūrvamākhyātaṃ lakṣapādādhike mate 
atra saṃkṣepataḥ prāptaṃ caturviṃśatsahasrake 
ṣoḍhānyāsasya sūtraṃ tu ākhyātaṃ tava sundara 
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye
kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasahitāyāṃ
avvākramabhāṣite ṣoḍhānyāsamañjūṣākramavarṇane
kramodayo nāmānandaḥ pañcaviṃśānandaḥ
śrīnātha uvāca'
kulaṃ ca 'ṣoḍaśairbhedairmayā' jñātaṃ maheśvari 
viparyāyeṇa' apara svābhāvikakula katham 
ṣaṭcakraṃ ṣoḍaśādhāraṃ trilakṣaṃ vyomapañcakam 
saṃsphuṭa ca na me jñātaṃ ' kulamārgakrameṇa tu 
idānīṃ kathyatām devi kulabhedaṃ yathā bhavet 
śrīvakrā uvāca 
etat praśna mahāśreṣṭhaṃ devadevāvatāritam 
vicāraṃ tasya vakṣyāmi kulapañcāśikākramam 
kulamūlakrama śambho śṛṇu vakṣyāmi bhairava 
adhomukhaṃ tu prathama kandanālasamudbhavam 
guptaṃ ta kandacakraṃ tu adhomukhavyavasthitam 
caturdalasamāyukta padmarāgasamaprabham 
catvārastasya bhedāśca ādhāre cakranāyakāḥ 
piṇḍaṃ tasya prasādaṃ tu himakundendunirmalam 
tasya ūdhve dvitīyaṃ ca yogarājamadhomukham 
vahnikapilasaṃkāśa jvālājvalitavigraham 
tasya bhedāḥ ṣaḍirjñeyā cakreśa svādhiṣṭhānakam 
tasya piṇḍa mahārāvaṃ ārakta śuddhavāsanam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tasya ūdhve tṛtīyaṃ tu cakraṃ nābhihutāśanam 
mahāratnaṃ mahādīptaṃ tasya bhedāni vai daśa 
svaraṣaṣṭhasamākrāntaṃ bindusaṃsthaśaśāṅkadhṛk 
dāḍimīkusumaprakhyaṃ jvalanta bhairavānalam 
ta piṇḍaṃ maṇipūrasya siddhasya iti niścayam 
cakranāyakavikhyāta surasiddhanamaskṛtam 
caturthaṃ tasya ūdhve tu hṛdi cakramadhomukham 
varṇaṃ taddvairikābhāsaṃ tasya bhedāni dvādaśa 
cakranāyakavikhyāta tatrānāhatabhairavam 
khecarīhṛdayaṃ tasya piṇḍa dvādaśavarṇakam 
dhyāna tasya bhaved raktamīṣadśyāmavimiśritam 
atova saṃpravakṣyāmi aparaṃ cakranirṇayam 
himakundendudhavala tasya bhedāni ṣoḍaśa 
viśuddhaṃ bhairavaṃ tatra kathitaṃ cakranāyakam 
tasya piṇḍa bhaved vāha tripadena vibheditam 
haritaṃ tasya varṇaṃ tu nīlajīmutasannibham 
tasyodhva paramaṃ cakraṃ turyasthānagataṃ pṛthu 
gokṣīrasadṛśānanda tejorūpaṃ bhagākṛtiḥ 
tasya bhedadvayaṃ proktaṃ ājñācakreśvaraṃ prabho 
vāgbhavaṃ tasya tat piṇḍaṃ sindūrāruṇasannibham 
ṣaṭtyāgāt saptamaṃ ūdhva ākāśe śūnyamaṇḍale 
turyātīta tu tat proktaṃ tasmāt ṣaṭka vinirgatam 
sṛṣṭikrameṇa ūdhvāddhi cakraughaṃ tat vibhāvyate 
kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
dvirāra turyacakraṃ tu kaṇṭhe vai ṣoḍaśārakam 
hṛdayaṃ dvādaśāraṃ tu nābhi daśabhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
ṣaḍāraṃ yonicakraṃ tu caturāra gudadaṃ smṛtam 
punaḥ siddhakramaṃ teṣāṃ viśuddhādikrameṇa tu 
viśuddhaṃ ṣoḍaśairbhedaiḥ dvādaśaistu anāhatam 
daśabhiśca maṇirbhinnaḥ svādhiṣṭhāna ṣaḍātmakam 
ādhāre bhedāścatvāra ājñā bhedadvayaṃ viduḥ 
akārādivisargāntā bhedāni ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ 
kakārādiṭhakārāntā dvādaśāni anāhate 
ḍakārādiphakārāntā bhedānāṃ daśakaṃ maṇau 
bakārādilakārānta bhedaṣaṭka krameṇa tu 
svādhiṣṭhāne  mahādeva ādhāre tu yathā śṛṇu 
vakārādisakārāntā bhedāścatvārādhāragāḥ 
ṣaṣṭhaṃ cakraṃ bhrūvormadhye hakṣadvayavinirmitam 
hakṣadvayavinirmuktāḥ ślokāni dvādaśaḥ smṛtāḥ 
ṣaṭtyāgāt saptame muktistatrānanda vyavasthitam 
aparaṃ ṣoḍaśādhārā lakṣatritayameva ca 
amṛtādivisargāntāḥ kalādhārāṇi ṣoḍaśa 
teṣāṃ ca yoginīsiddhāḥ svaśarīre vyavasthitāḥ 
ananta caiva ākāśaṃ induḥ īśvarasaṃjñakam 
udayaṃ ūrjanāthaṃ ca ṛkṣakarṇaṃ ca ṛṣabham 
liptāṅgaṃ lūlihaścaiva ekapādaṃ maheśvara 
tathā vai rāvaṇo nāma ovalī nāma aumuniḥ 
ambunāthaṃ ahvavāha ādhārā ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
ete caiva mahāsiddhā ādyante aisamāyutāḥ 
etaistu vyāpitaṃ piṇḍaṃ teṣā sthānāni ṣoḍaśa 
prathama ghaṇṭikāyā tu dvitīyaṃ tālumaṇḍale 
majje mede tathā śukre anyaccaiva tu kuṇḍalī
snāyvasthitvacaromāṇi kesara ca tathāmṛtam 
māṃsa ca rudhiraṃ caiva vāḍavānala mārutam 
ākāśaṃ ca tathā deva evamādhāraṣoḍaśa 
teṣāṃ olitrayaṃ deva sattvarajastamastrayam
lakṣatraya samāsena mano buddhirahaṃkṛtiḥ 
teṣāṃ vai trīṇi siddhāśca kūṭasthā oṣamitra
eteṣā tu laya deva pañcavyomastu bhairava 
ādhāre hṛdaye caiva tathā kule kapāṭake 
pañcavyomagataṃ lakṣa bhittvā caiva tu khegatiḥ 
somamaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ aparaṃ sūryamaṇḍalam 
vāyumaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ aparaṃ vyomamaṇḍalam 
ākāśaṃ pañcadhā proktaṃ adho madhye ca mūrdhani 
eteṣāṃ vyāpakāḥ pañca bindumārgaprabhedakāḥ 
śivādyantasamāyuktaṃ teṣāṃ vai siddhapañcakam 
pṛthivyāpastathā tejo vāyurākāśameva ca 
ete pañca mahābhūtā nirmitā sṛṣṭikārakāḥ 
śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śaṅkaro'nantaḥ sādākhya piṅgalastathā 
pañcaite sṛṣṭikartāra siddhāḥ pañcakule tathā 
śrīkaṇṭhaḥ pṛthivī jñeyaḥ śaṅkaroṃ āpa ucyate 
tejo'nanta iti proktaḥ sādākhyo vāyurucyate 
ākāśa piṅgalo jñeyaḥ pañcaite sṛṣṭikārakāḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
etad vai kulamārga tu tavākhyātaṃ rahasyakam 
guptā kulavadhū yadvat tadvad gopyataraṃ kulam 
uddhāraṃ pūrvato jñātvā paścād yajanamārabhet 
etat kulakramācāra bindumaṇḍalabheditam 
tatra lakṣe mati kṛtvā rudraśakti pravartate 
adho madhye ca ūdhve vā ātmatulyādhikārakam' 
kuryāccaiva svadehasya cittaṃ damayateṃ tataḥ 
bahirantarabhāvena tadā cotpadyate sukham 
tatkulākulamādāya  śarīraṃ ṣaṭkabheditam  
navasaṃjña punarbhūyaḥ kulabhedārṇavaṃ bhavet 
śaṅkha śaktistathā yoga mahāgṛha caturthakam 
pañcamaṃ ca prabhu proktaṃ pādaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhamucyate 
atītamāvalī caiva uttarau parikīrtitau
tasyottamaṃ mahādeva ānanda navamaṃ kulam 
kulaṃ tu navadhā bhinnaṃ vikhyātaṃ sarvatomukham 
uḍḍāmara siddhakaula gaṇākhya khecarīmatam 
candrākhya rauravaṃ deva vīrākhya bhūtaḍāmaram 
navamaṃ tu mahākaula pratyayaṃ svādhikārakam 
tenāvatāritā cājñā lakṣapādādhike mate 
tasmāt tat siddhakaula  tu tadā kaulasya pratyayam'
avasthā unmanī bhāva etat kaulopadeśakam 
kulakaula samākhyātaṃ ādyānta tamanāhata 
kulamekaṃ vijānīyāt  vyomapañcakabheditam  
āsanaṃ bhedanaṃ teṣāṃ kulapañcāśikākramam kumārikākhaṇḍa
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede
ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākrama
bhāṣitekulapañcāśikādhikāravarṇane kramodayo
nāmānandaḥ 
śrinātha uvāca
ṣaḍviṃśānandaḥ
kiṃ kula kiṃkramācāra kā pūjā kramamaṇḍale 
kathayasva maheśāni prasādād vada me prabho 
śrīvakrā uvāca
kramādyaṃ mūlasūtra tu vṛttādhyuṣṭapramāṇataḥ 
tasyārabhya' kramāt sṛṣṭi ityā  khecaram 
yā' sā śaktirbhagākhyā trividhagatiyutā tryakṣarā triprakārā
tasyā śrī oḍḍiyāṇa parakalasahita madhyasthaṃ sudīptam 
tacchrījālandharākhyaṃ prakaṭitanilaya dakṣiṇe caiva koṇe
vāme śrīpūrṇapīṭha paśujanabhayakṛt kāmarūpaṃ tada
tasyodhve tisrapīṭha paramakalayutaṃ candrapīṭhaṃ lalāṭe
trikoṇānte samastaṃ paramaśivakalākṣobhita divyama
tanmadhye vakraliṅga paramasukhakara bindurūpaṃ tribhinna
nityānandasvarūpa taduparimathanāt  ṣaṭprakārādhikāram 
a
pūrvāmnāyakramaugha tadupari aparaṃ vṛddhakaumārabālam
evaṃ vyāptaṃ samastaṃ sthitilayajananī rudraśaktistribhedaiḥ kumārikākhaṇḍa
ciñcājñā kādibhedairakulakulamayānandadā bodharūpā 
guvajñā ṣaṭkārā paśubhayaharaṇī candrabimbasya madhye 
nityaklinnā suraktābhayamuditaparānandaśakti prasiddhā
kurvantī śāmbhavauṣa kṣubhitavaratanuḥ śrīkujā divyaliṅgam 
mayāvatārita  tubhyamādyasūtramadhomukham
yā sā śakti parākhyātā sā ca devī bhagākṛtiḥ 
tasyānte sā parā devī pīṭhānāṃ pīṭhadevatā 
yā sā śaktirbhagākhyātā gatistasyāstridhā punaḥ 
ādikādithakārādibrahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ 
jyeṣṭhā vāmā ca raudrī ca dvādaśaślokabheditāḥ 
parā sā rudraśaktistu tribhiḥ sthānaivyavasthitā 
lalāṭe hṛdaye yonau kṣarate triṣu kāriṣu 
śukraṃ ca śoṇitaṃ kṛcchra nāḍītritayasandhiṣu 
iḍā ca piṅgalā caiva suṣumnā madhyamā trayaḥ 
evamānandayogena triśakti svādhikārikā 
tasyāyāta kramaṃ deva bālakaumāravṛddhakam 
pīṭhapañcakasaṃyukta kramameka trayoliṣu 
ānandānandabinduśca akṣara  paramā kalā 
pīṭhānyete kramāt pañca antaraṅge pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
bahiraṅge ca te kūṭā ojāpūkā ca tisrakam 
samastaṃ ca kula kaulaṃ śivaśaktikalāvṛtam 
ānandāvṛtavṛndastu ānande tu pravartate 
udbhavānandacittasya samatvaṃ ca pravartate 
tanmadhye sūkṣmaliṅga tu divyaliṅgamadhomukham 
paramākāśamadhyastha candramaṇḍalamadhyataḥ 
tadā tat suṣira yāti lakṣitenāntarātmanā 
paśyate tu samādhistho bindurūpaṃ nabhastalam 
cidānandasamutpatti āveśa saṃpravartate 
tadrūpaṃ ca svarūpaṃ ca ityāśrāvaṇapratyayam 
mathite cittacaitanye mathitaṃ karmasaṃśrayam  
mathanādapi cakrasya yogāveśa muhurmuhuḥ 
ārakta tatkule cakraṃ tatrasthaṃ bindumaṇḍalam 
bheditaṃ drāvita yasmāt mathitaṃ smaraṇena tu 
ṣaṭprakārairvibhinna tu bhedaiścaivāṣṭaviṃśatiḥ 
catuṣkaṃ pañcaka ṣaṭka catuṣkaṃ pañcaka catuḥ 
ṣaṭprakārakrama hyetat yo vetti sa ca kaulikaḥ  
ādau pīṭhacatuṣkaṃ tu catvāraḥ pīṭhadevatā  
siddhapañcakamanya tu jñānaṣaṭkasamanvitam 
mahantārīpañcaka ca olitrayakulakramam 
aṣṭāviṃśatibhirbhedaiḥ prakārāṇi ṣaḍi smṛtāḥ
kumārikākhaṇḍa
etairbhinna kulātmāna tadā ānandasantatiḥ 
kalisyānte ca kāmākhye samīpasthaṃ ca pañcakam 
avasthā ca kule kaule tisrākhye jāyate hi ca 
sa cāṣṭāviṃśamo bhedo bhaviṣye ca bhaviṣyati 
evaṃ te pañcabhiḥ pīṭhā pūrvasūtre visarpitā 
tathā ca devatādīni sṛṣṭinyāye ataḥ śṛṇu 
gajajihvā agnijihvā taḍijjihvā tṛtīyakā 
śukrajihvā ca amarā rasajihvā ca pañcamī 
teṣāṃ siddhī kramāt pañca idānī pravadāmyaham 
candrārkānalabimbastha bindau ca gaṇapañcakam 
āveśa ghūrṇirānandaḥ ūṣmā kroṣaṇaśoṣaṇam 
etad vai jñānaṣaṭkaṃ tu prakṛtisthaṃ prameyataḥ 
māyā ca śāmbhavī śakti icchā jñānī kriyā tathā 
etaccatuṣkamākhyāta pañcakaṃ mahantārikā 
śabdā spaśī rasā devī rūpavyāpī ca gandhinī 
ete vai tvadahaṃkāryā pañcaka parikīrtitam 
vimalāntaramātmāna evaṃ olitrika smṛtam 
eva te kramabhedāni kathitānyaṣṭaviṃśatiḥ 
etairbhinnaṃ mahāliṅgaṃ divyamaṇḍalasaṃjñakam 
teṣāṃ vidyānvaya yacca parā sā paramā kalā kumārikākhaṇḍa
nityoditā susūkṣmā ca nāsāgre saṃvyavasthitā 
ūrṇatantunibhākārā gokṣīrahimaśītalā 
tayāsau jīvate jīvo divyaliṅgaṃ maheśvara 
tasya siddhānvayaṃ sarvaṃ bhedāñcaivāṣṭaviṃśatiḥ 
tayā prāśitamātrā yā antarbhavaḥ pravartate 
trināḍisaṃgama sthūlaṃ ekatra yatra tiṣṭhati 
tena ta tripuraṃ pīṭhaṃ tribhiḥ srotapravāhakam 
tisrākhya ca lalāṭastha brahmagranthiradhomukhī
lalāṭasuṣira cakraṃ pratyaya jñānaraśmayaḥ 
evaṃ vyāptaṃ krama meroryoginī ca adhomukhī 
sā śakti paramā tatra sthitā viśrāmakāriṇī 
dakṣiṇottarayoḥ pārrave jananī calate pure 
bhagamadhyamaśṛṅgasya tasyāgre tu layaṃ punaḥ 
evaṃ sā rudraśaktistu tribhirbhedaiḥ pratiṣṭhitā 
ādisthāne sthitā tatra devadevī kulecchayā 
dadate jñānasadbhāvaṃ kuṭilāṅgī svatantrataḥ 
tadānandaḥ pravarteta  mokṣamārgamahotsava 
ājñā gurumukhād labdhvā rudraśaktiḥ pravartate 
vaktrād vaktragatā ājñā bandhubhūtā kulakrame 
vācāsiddhi kule kaule bhavanāt saṃpravartate 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
karmaṇā manasā vācā triśuddhirbhaktivatsale 
tasyājñā vartate śiṣye bhāvahīno na siddhyati 
paśupāśabhaya  śiṣye anyathā ca bhaved dhruvam 
rudraśaktirmahādevī amoghā ca jagatsutā 
divyājñāyā svarūpā sā siddharūpā tvanekadhā 
nityaklinnāprabhāvena atiraktasvarūpataḥ 
udayaṃ labhate śiṣya paramānandalakṣaṇam 
pratirūpā ca yā śaktiḥ prasiddhā cchāyajā parā 
kurvantī nitya karmāṇi manecchayā  yathā sudhīḥ 
mocayecchakticakrastho  divyaliṅganurdharaḥ 
candrādityajale cchāyā agnisomārkadarpaṇe 
tathā sā tārakānte ca parā devī susūkṣmagā 
paśudharā yathā paśyet kuṭilā ca adhomukhīm
sā ca devī hyahaṃ mūrtiḥ kubjikā kulakaulinī 
tasyāḥ sūtrakramaṃ coktaṃ kramaogha vinirgatam 
prajñārthaṃ saṃgataṃ paśyenmūlasūtropadeśakam  
ityāgamaviśuddhasya prajñāsūtramaya hara 
malasyaivopaghātārthaṃ nirṇītāmiha saṃhitām 
anena sūcitaṃ sūtra mūlasūtraṃ tu mūlataḥ 
prajñāsūtravinirmukto yo'nyathā avadhārayet 
na tasya sūtraṃ na mūlaṃ tu na jñānaṃ jñeyarūpataḥ 
na kulaṃ ca kramaṃ naiva nācārya naiva putrakam 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena mūlasūtraṃ samāyet 
śrīnātha uvāca
kramaugha mūlasūtraṃ tu prajñāsūtreṇa bodhitam 
tvanmukhācca mayā jñātaṃ siddho'haṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ 
divyānandaprakāśo'yaṃ utpannastvatprasādataḥ
kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
aiṃ namo'stu te mahāmāye ajite tejarūpiṇi 
somamaṇḍalamadhyasthe nādarūpe khamāśrite
aiṃkāravigrahāvasthe divyaliṅge napuṃsake 
kalisyāṃ parame māto ante ambe kulamba 
ādipīṭhasamudbhūte pañcāśatpīṭhamāśrite 
vahnikapilasaṃkāśe sphurannāḍīprabodhake 
visargānte samudbhūte vāgbhave parameśvari 
hakārārdhakalādhāre śūnyabhūte khagodite
bindusthe caiva candrasthe khecarīcakramāśrite 
devīnāṃ gurumānāmbe kubjike parameśvari 
īśvarāntargate māta ātmānandavibhedite 
kūṭasthe devadeveśi yogapīṭhe vyavasthite 
durgamārgodite bhīme maṇḍalānte kalau yuge 
āvarte ca nirāvarte laye viśrāmakāriṇi 
maṅgalā tvaṃ mahādevi oṃkārapīṭhamāśrite 
devi jālandhare māye pūrṇapīṭhe adhomukhi 
tvaṃ ca kāmeśvarī klinne yoginī kāmarūpake 
māyā tvaṃ bhairavīśaktinīyakī pīṭhapañcake 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
kālī tvaṃ caiva ujjainyā ardhapīṭheśvareśvarīṃ 
tvaṃ ca pīṭhopapīṭheṣu tvamādyā kramamaṇḍale 
pañcapraṇavamadhyasthe pūrṇānte kulamātare 
mātṛcakrasthite devi ṣaḍyoginiparāvṛte 
tvaṃ ca sā ḍākinī māyā aprameyātitejasā 
kiṅkiṇī jvālaghoṣāṇāṃ vīṇāpaṭadundu 
tridhāmadhāmasaṃghaṭṭe tridhāgatisamāśrite 
triprakāragate śānte mātṛmantratanupriye 
aiṃkārāsanamārūḍhe bindurūpe tridhāgate 
hrīkārajanani devi kṣā kṣā klīṃkārabhedani
vyāpaki vyāptivarṇānāṃ yārālāvānivāsini 
hemahemāvati devi hasini haṃsamadhyage 
haṃsanādeśvari bhīme vadehe adhomukhi 
subhage vimale śānte prameyajñānavallabhe
kumārikākhaṇḍa
brahmarūpasvarūpe ca aiṃ hrīṃ śrīṃ samayāvṛte 
hrīṃkāratriguṇāvarte hrī hrī mantratanu priye 
māyārūpadharīdevi gajajihve gajeśvari 
tvameva vidyujjihvā ca hā hrī hū ca bhagodbhave 
bhavodbhave bhavātīte turyastheturyamūrdhani 
praśāntapadamārūḍhe ṣaṭtyāgāt saptameśvari 
sūkṣme caiva susūkṣme ca susthite ca surādhipe 
ānande ca nirānande amarīkramabhūṣite 
glakāre pārthive brāhmī slūkāre tvaṃ ca vaiṣṇavī 
plakāre tvaṃ kule raudrī mlakāre tvaṃ ca īśvarī 
nlūkāre nāyakī nandā nityānandapare ratā 
māyā tvaṃ sarvasiddhīnāṃ pīṭhānāṃ saṃsthitā ume 
me māte parame māye me śive me sarasvati 
me mātā me ca me bhāyī me ca jīvāntarālaye 
prabhu divyaśaktistvaṃ ārakte tattvavāsase 
sarvāṅgasundari klinne jīvanāḍigate śubhe 
hāhrīhūkāramantraistu calase syanda jagat 
mantrāveśapade gauri śaktyante ca samāśrite 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
kulamātaṅginīcakre vidyādevīti kubja 
pūrṇacandranibhākāre candrapūrṇabhagānane  
saptāviṃśapadairbhedaiḥ aṣṭāviṃśatpadodbhave 
cakranāyaki kaulīśe īśvarīkulamāśrite 
siddhapañcāśarūpeṇa kamale kamaleśvari 
aṭṭahāsasamudbhūte haṃsamaṇḍalabhūṣite 
somamaṇḍalamadhyasthe māyā tvaṃ sūryamaṇḍale 
tvamagnimaṇḍalāntasthe dīptajihve maheśvari 
vāyuvege manāntasthe parāparavisarpite 
śūnye śūnyāntarāvasthe māruti siddhasevite 
nirālambe gate devi ākāśe duratikrame 
jñānavijñānagambhīre jñeyarūpe ca kevale 
sthitilayakarīdevi janani tattvamaṇḍale 
tattvānā kṣobhaṇī śakti ajñānatamabhedanī 
mātarī sarvadevānāṃ mama prāṇapriye ume 
viśveśvarī jagaddhātrī saṃpradāyapradāyinī
namaste paranirvāṇe jagadyonimahāmbike 
smara tvaṃ samayaṃ pūrvaṃ snehena manavigraham 
tuṣṭā bhava pare'smākaṃ mātā  tvaṃ tridaśairapi 
iti māyāstava  proktaṃ yogīvāṇīkramāgatam 
tasyāvatāraṃ kurute vakrikā pīṭhadevatā kumārikākhaṇḍa
sukhamārogyasaṃpattimavasthā labhate naraḥ 
sarvapāpavinirmukto bhavate tatkṣaṇādapi 
na tasya punarāvṛttimīyāstavamudīraṇāt 
ihaiva prāpnuyād bhogān lābha pūjāyaśa śriyaḥ 
avasthā kramayuktasya pāramparyeṇa tasya ca 
samayācārayuktasya tīvrājñā saṃpravartate 
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye
kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasra
saṃhitāyāṃ avvākramabhāṣite mūlasūtrādhikāravarṇane
māyāstavādhikāro nāmānandaḥ 
saptaviṃśānandaḥ
śrīnātha uvāca
devi siddhe' jagatsvāmi' ādināthe kulodbhave 
brūhi jñānopadeśaṃ tu yat sāraṃ paścimānvaye 
prakaṭaṃ kuru kaulīśe pūjāāgamamaṇḍalam' 
śrīvakrā uvāca
sāraṃ śaivasya jagato bhuvanākṛtimaṇḍalam 
bāhyasthaṃ ca svadehasthaṃ antaraṅgaṃ cidātmakam 
tadahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi' gurumaṇḍalakaṃ yathā 
yo'sau anādiravyakta  śivaḥ paramakāraṇaḥ 
mantramūrtirabhūnnātha' lokānugrahahetunā 
avatīrṇastu bhūloke anugrahakaraḥ paraḥ 
pūjyo'sau maṇḍale deva navātmānandabhairavaḥ 
pañcamūrtidharo nātha ṣoḍaśāvayavānvitaḥ 
navadhāmūrtimāśritya avatīrṇaḥ kalau yuge 
pañcāśadrudramūrtisthoṃ yathā pūjyastathā śṛṇu 
tasyoddhāra mahādeva ślokaiḥ pañcabhiḥ sūcitam  
akāre catvare madhye pañcamaṃ ca tathā punaḥ 
lakayakṣatana ramaḍakha ceti viparyayet 
ḍa ḍha ṭha ṭa daparyantaṃ sṛṣṭyā merorvinirgatam 
maṇḍalaṃ taṃ smṛtaṃ deva dvitīyaṃ cādhikārayoḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
indra āpastathā tejo vāyurākāśameva ca 
jñānogya  kuṇḍalī koṭi tṛtīyā varavarṇini 
hṛdaya samaya caiva sarvajñaṃ ca kadambakam 
khagīśaṃ gurunāthaṃ ca ratnabījaṃ caturthakam 
kadamba vimalaugha ca samayaṃ bhairavāvalī 
pādukānte manu smṛtvā pūjayed gurumaṇḍalam 
vidyāpīṭhāgrato deva gurumaṇḍalapūjanam 
pūrvakrama yathā coktaṃ pañcāsanasamanvitam 
prasādatrayasabhinnaṃ arcayet guru pañcadhā 
īśakoṇāt samārabhya yāvanmadhyaṃ tu pañcamam 
maṇḍalaṃ cādhikāra ca siddhāḥ samaya yoginī 
pañcadhā pañcabhirbhinna pañcadhākaulinīyutam 
vāgbhavaṃ māyayā sārdhaṃ lakṣmīprasādabheditam 
navātmānandasaṃyuktaṃ pañcabhirgurumaṇḍalam 
pādukāntaṃ mahādeva pūjayet satataṃ varam 
antaraṅgagatāḥ pūjyā maṇḍalāni tathātmani 
ādhāre prathamaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyaṃ yonimaṇḍale 
tṛtīyaṃ nābhicakre tu caturtha ca anāhate 
pañcamaṃ kaṇṭhadeśe tu ādināthaṃ tu mūrdhani 
śrīkaṇṭhādi piṅgalānta pañcadhā pañca kalpitam 
prabhāte caiva madhyāhne sandhyākāle tu sundara 
vidyāpīṭhāgrataḥ kuryāt guroragre tu pañcadhā 
ārādhanaṃ tu kartavyaṃ saṃpūrṇa siddhidaṃ bhavet 
na rikta maṇḍalaṃ kuryāt gurora kadācana 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
yathāvittānusāreṇa kṛtvā saṃpūrṇapūjanam 
ārātrī candanaṃ dīpa vīradravyasamanvitam 
nivedana prakartavyaṃ sāṣṭāṅga ca namaskaret 
tridhā ca pañcadhā caiva sāṣṭāṅga daṇḍavat sudhīḥ 
pradakṣiṇaśataṃ kṛtvā pūjayed gurupādukām 
etadācārasamaya pālayet satataṃ budhaḥ 
pālanād bhavate siddhiḥ anyathā narakaṃ vrajet 
oliparveṣu sarveṣu nityanaimittikeṣu ca 
maṇḍalakramapūjāyāṃ sarva saṃpūrṇatāṃ vrajet 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu bhairava tattvataḥ 
śrīkramaṃ tu tataḥ pūjya yathoktaṃ śrīkulāgame 
tasyāvatāraṃ saṃkṣepāt paryaṅke satataṃ kuru 
mṛgājine tu saṃkalpya āsane vāgbhavaṃ śubham 
śrīkhaṇḍacandanaṃ śuddha kaṃkumaṃ cālimiśritam 
abhimantrya ca vidyāyāḥ kramaṃ likhya tridhāvidham 
ādyakramasya vṛddhasya yogapīṭhaṃ tridhoditam 
tadbāhye likhya ṣaṭkoṇa aiṃkāreṇa tu veṣṭayet 
aṣṭāraṃ padmaka bāhye mekhalātritayāvṛtam 
catuṣkoṇa tu tadbāhye likhya ca susūtritam 
ṣaṭkoṇacakrasaṃyukta  kaumārasya kramaṃ likhet 
aṣṭārapadmasaṃyukta  krama bālakramasya ca 
evaṃ te kramabhedo'ya maṇḍalasya prakāśitam kumārikākhaṇḍa
nyāsabhedaṃ yathā  deva vṛddhakaumārabālake 
prathama śabdarāśistu dvitīyā mālinī tathā 
vidyātritayamevaṃ tu tadaṅgāni caturthakam 
aghoryaṣṭakamevaṃ tu tathā siddhāṅgapañcakam 
ṣoḍhānyāsamidaṃ kṛtvā paścād yajanamārabhet 
vṛddhakramasya jyeṣṭhasya nyāsāvaraṇamuttamam 
atha madhyamasiddhasya kaumārasya yathākramam 
prathamaṃ tadgraha kṣetraṃ dvitīyaṃ bījapañcakam 
dvādaśāṅgaṃ tṛtīyaṃ ca siddhāṅgaṃ ca caturthakam 
pañcamaṃ tu ṣaḍaṅgaṃ syāt pīṭhanyāsaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhakam 
khecara saptamaṃ nāma kṛtvā yajanamārabhet 
atha tṛtīyakaṃ vakṣye kramasyāvaraṇa punaḥ 
prathamā samayā vidyā siddhāṅgaṃ ca dvitīyakam 
tṛtīyaṃ tu ṣaḍaṅgaṃ syāt ślokāni tu caturthakam 
pañcamaṃ cādhikāra syāt ṣaṣṭhaṃ kṣetraparigraham 
saptamaṃ ratnavinyāsaṃ vidyānyāsaṃ tathāṣṭamam 
evaṃ nyāsakramaṃ nyasya paścād bālakramaṃ yajet 
kramāṇāṃ maṇḍalaṃ jñātvā ekacakre tu paścime 
siddhāṅgaṃ ca ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ca dvāvetau tu viśodhayet kumārikākhaṇḍa
viśvāmitrakapālaṃ tu susiddhaṃ yogināṃ śubham 
pīṭhāgre dravyasaṃpūrṇa vratīnāṃ nṛkapālakam 
koṅkaṇāstreṇa saṃśodhya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
mūrti praviśya hṛdaye netre ṣaṇmukhamāharet 
śikhāsānnidhyakaraṇaṃ saṃpūrṇaṃ tu śireṇa tu 
evaṃ ṣaḍvidhasaṃskāra mūlavidyā niyojayet 
yonimudrā mahāmudrā tayāsa mudrito bhavet 
avatāraṃ tato deva karālākhya niyojayet 
mūlavidyā tridhā japtvā sānnidhyaṃ kramamaṇḍale 
aparaṃ dvitīya pātra candanāmṛtapūritam 
pañcakādyena saṃsthāpya punastenābhimantritam 
atha tṛtīyakaṃ pātraṃ sthāpita ratnapañcake 
tena yaṣṭvā punastatra dakṣiṇottaramadhyataḥ 
evaṃ pātratrayaṃ pūrvaṃ kṛtvā pūjā samārabhet 
candanena tu vinyāsaṃ vidyāyā ātmasantatau 
bhakārādicakārāntaṃ sthāne sthāne pṛthak pṛthak 
ātmānaṃ dhūpitaṃ kuryād vinyāsaṃ mūlavidyayā 
aṅganyāsa samārabhya sva  olyā tu yathākramam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tilatailāṣṭadīpāni pañcādyena pradīpayet 
digvidikṣu ca pīṭhasya adhivāsamanantaram 
candanaṃ dhūpasaugandhakuṃkumākṣatasaṃyutam 
mūlamantrasya siddhasya kuryād dāna ca santatau 
mudrātritayaṃ kṛtvādau tataḥ pūjāṃ samārabhet 
pūrvakrameṇa kartavyaṃ dehasthaṃ kramapūjanam 
paścād bāhye tu pīṭhasthaṃ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ kramam 
candanākṣatasaṃmiśrairādau kuryāt kramārcanam 
śvetapuṣpaiḥ sugandhaiśca taistu pūjyaṃ kulakramam 
abhāvād raktapuṣpaistu tathā pītaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ 
sumanācampakaiḥ padyaistathā nīlotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
deśācāreṇa labdhaistu taistu pūjyaṃ kulakramam 
nirgandhaiśca sakaṇṭakairbhagnai saṃkucitairdumaiḥ 
kramapūjā na kartavyā manasāpi sureśvara 
dhūpārcanaṃ punaścaiva pṛthak ājñākramaṃ punaḥ 
alipūjā tataḥ kāryā vaiṣṇavīpadamātrataḥ 
pratyaya vyākulaṃ tatra mahārāva pravartate 
sānnidhyamatulaṃ cograṃ paśūnāṃ ca bhayāvaham 
mūlamantreṇa vidyāyā vāmapāṇyakṣasūtrakam 
sphāṭikaṃ putrajīvaṃ vā mātrā aṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ 
dvimātrāṃ vā trimātrā vā icchayā vā manīṣiṇām 
sthūla vā sūkṣmamaṇi vā na meru laṅghayet kvacit 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
aṃguṣṭa varjayitvā tu yathā prāpta catuṣṭayam 
madhyamau dvau tathā varjayau vāmāvartaparibhramāt 
etat pāṇikṛtaṃ japyaṃ akṣasūtreṇa vā kṛtam 
cūlāgramamalaṃ śuddhaṃ uparisthamakṣamālayā 
taṃ ca meruṃ vijānīyāllaṅghanānnarakaṃ vrajet 
vāmāvartakrameṇaiva sadyojātaṃ vidhīyate 
tadārūhya paraṃ dhyānaṃ mantra vāpi ca muktidam 
svaolyāmātmapīṭhasya ātmānamaṇḍale'pi vā 
mantratriṣkoṇamadhye tu athavā pūrṇavidyāyām 
dvicatvāriṃśatsaṃjñāyā japyaṃ dhyānaṃ trikoṇake 
kuryāt tanmānasaṃ japyaṃ ātmakūṭamathāpi vā 
mudritaṃ yonimudrāyāmamānāmāṅkita śivam 
ādau tanmūlavidyāyā agnikuṇḍasya madhyataḥ 
dhyānamāraktakṛṣṇaṃ tu kuryāt karmānurūpataḥ 
ūdhvamadhyamadhaḥ kuryāt saṃskāraṃ ca tathā puna 
mama yonigataṃ dhyāyenna bāhye viniyojayet 
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye kādibhede
ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasaṃhitāyāṃ avvākrama
bhāṣite kramamaṇḍalagurumaṇḍalādhikāravarṇane
kramodayo nāmānandaḥ śrīnātha uvāca
śrutaṃ devi mayā sarvaṃ pūjāvidhi' yathākramam 
adhunā śrotumicchāmi kramamekaṃ tridhā' kathaṃ 
śrīvakrā uvāca
aṣṭāviṃśānandaḥ
śṛṇu nātha pravakṣyāmi kramamekaṃ tridhā yathā 
olitritayabhedena bālakaumāravṛddha 
vṛddhakramaṃ tu prathamaṃ jyeṣṭha  olikramāgatam' 
mantriṇātu yathā deva āyātaṃ jñānanirṇayam 
pīṭhānāmādyavarṇāśca ojāpūkācatuṣṭayam 
te yugāni catvāraste pīṭhāni aihikībhuvi 
te ca pañcamahābhūtāścatuvyāpakasaṃyutāḥ 
oṃ kārādikrameṇaiva vyomatattvāditaḥ kramāt 
oṃkāra vyomatattvasthaṃ jākāra  tejasi sthitam 
pūkāramāpatattvastha kākāra  pṛthivīgatam 
kuryācchaktimadhasteṣāṃ
teṣāmadhogataṃ pārtha
adhaḥśaktyāṅgasaṃsthayā 
āpo daṇḍaśca mālinī 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
evaṃ pīṭhāścaturbhinnā lāñchitā candrasūryayoḥ 
ājñā mūrdhni kṛtā hyeṣā khyātā pīṭhacatuṣṭayam 
teṣāṃ caturvidhaṃ dhyānaṃ vakṣye ātmagataṃ priya 
aghorasadṛśodhā jākāra puruṣaṃ viduḥ 
pūkāraṃ vāmadevaṃ tu kākāra sadyarūpakam 
antaraṅge sthitā devyo bhrūmadhye hṛdi nābhigāḥ 
yonimadhye samākhyātāsteṣu devyācatuṣṭayam 
kakārādiṣu catvāraḥ strīnapuṃsakabheditāḥ 
pīṭheśvarya samākhyātā pīṭhadhyānasamāyutāḥ 
teṣu siddhāñca catvāraḥ pūjyā pīṭhacatuṣṭaye 
haraśabdaścatunyāsa haraśabdaścatuṣṭayam 
ādyadīrgheścaturbhinna ājñāyā śikharāṅkitam 
pīṭhabījāśca catvāraḥ dhyānaṃ teṣāṃ ca pūrvavat 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vyomapañcakanirṇayam 
vyoma tu pañcadhā sthāpya śaktyādhastejabṛṃhitam 
dīrghapañcakasaṃbhinnaṃ bindunādairalaṃkṛtam 
vyomapañcakametaddhi dhyānaṃ teṣāmaghoravat 
ājñāsaṃkrāmaka deva tasya mantrakramaṃ bhavet 
ye coktā  vyāpakā pañca tejorūpā mahābalāḥ 
teṣāṃ sthānāni vai pañca asmin śāstre pracakṣmahe 
śrotre nāsāpuṭe vaktre jñātavyaṃ vyomapañcakam 
pṛthivī cāpatattvaṃ tu tejo vāyuḥ khasaṃjñakam 
śaktitattvaṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ teṣāṃ caivādho raviḥ kumārikākhaṇḍa
tathā tad vāyutattvaṃ ca nādākṣaravibheditam 
bindusthaṃ nādaśaktisthaṃ ājñākūṭaṃ maheśvara 
gude yonau tathā nābhau hṛdi kaṇṭhe bhruvontare 
eteṣāṃ kathitaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ saṃketena ca ṣaḍvidham 
śvetā ca prathamā vartirdvitīyā pītarūpinī 
tṛtīyā nīlavaṇī ca caturthī haritā bhavet 
pañcamā gairikābhā ca ṣaṣṭhī āraktavarṇikā 
pañcaka cāpara vakṣye mahantāyī manoharam 
haṃseti pañcadhā sthāpya a i u e osamanvitam 
nādaśaktisamākrānta mahantāryaśca pañcakam 
kukṣibhyā stanayormadhye kuryāt pṛṣṭhe'pi kārakaṃ 
śveta pītaṃ ca āraktaṃ harita gaṇapañcakam 
dhyāna vai pañcadhā teṣāṃ trikamadhye  yathā bhavet 
trikaṇṭakaṃ samākhyātaṃ vidyātritayamabhyaset 
ādhāre hṛdaye tūrye teṣāṃ sthānatraya bhavet 
ārakta prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ dvitīyaṃ pītakaṃ bhavet 
tṛtīya śuddhadhavala sattvarājasatāmasam 
saptāviṃśatibhedaistu mantrakrama samuddhṛtam 
tasya saṃjñākramaṃ vakṣye sāmprataṃ śṛṇu bhairava 
ojāpūkācatuṣka tu kāpūjāocatuṣṭayam 
prakaṭa pīṭhadevasya mantrapīṭhe nirantaram 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
teṣāṃ vai guptanāmāni avimete asaṃjñayā 
mantradevyastato deva teṣāṃ nāmacatuṣṭayam 
samameti ca sākāra iti devyāḥ parigraham 
upadeśavaśenaiva pīṭhadevyāḥ samarcayet 
vyomapañcakamevaṃ tu mantrayuktaṃ samabhyaset 
teṣāṃ vai devatā   pañca pūjākāle pracakṣma 
vyoma tu pañcadhā kuryāt teṣāṃ pañcādhikārakam 
kāsirephasiye pañcasaṃyogād vyomapañcakam 
tataścājñā bhavet ṣaṭkaṃ guptā saṃjñā kramasya vai 
ājñākukārasabhinnaṃ ṣaḍvidha ca niyojayet 
teṣvagre saṃgatā devyo adhikārakrame sthitāḥ 
lavarahayaśa ṣaḍbhi  saṃketāñca prakīrtitāḥ 
tathā siddhāśca catvāraḥ pūrvoktakramasaṃyutāḥ 
asantatisu pañcaitāsteṣā guptābhidhānakam 
viṣuva saṃkramaṇānta anādipañcakṣetrakam 
trika trikaṇṭakādīni vidyātritayabhūṣitam 
ekāra ca akāraṃ ca kakāra ca tṛtīyakam 
eṣāṃ guptābhidhānāni ku ku ku devatātrayam 
catuṣkaṃ pañcakaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ catuṣkaṃ pañcakaṃ trikam 
etāni ṣaṭprakārāṇi bhedāni saptaviṃśatiḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
ādau pīṭhacatuṣkaṃ tu catvāraḥ pīṭhadevatā 
vyomapañcakamanya tu ājñāṣaṭka tathāparam 
punaḥ siddhacatuṣkaṃ tu anādiriti pañcakam 
trikaṇṭaka tathā vācya jyeṣṭha  olikramoddhṛtam 
etad vṛddhakramākhyātaṃ pañcapraṇavadīpitam 
sthānamantrasamāyuktaṃ dhyānadhāraṇasaṃyutam 
dehastha pūjayed yastu sa bhavet kulayogina  
jyeṣṭha  olikramākhyātaṃ pūjitavyaṃ tu deśikaiḥ 
vidyāpīṭhāt samārabhya krama pūjya yathārthataḥ 
upadeśavaśenaiva labdhvā gurumukhād yajet 
anyathā vighnadā cakre gurorājñā na laṅghayet 
atha dvitīyaka vakṣye kaumāra madhyamolikam  
vṛddhakrame  krameṇaiva upadeśayutaṃ yathā 
pūrṇapīṭhāt samārabhya madhyamolyā kramārcanam 
teṣāṃ nāmāni varṇāśca tattvayuktā manīṣiṇām 
śaktyādhiṣṭhitacatvāra haramāyāsanasthitāḥ 
ā  īū aisvarairbhinnā nādabindukalāṅkitā 
evaṃ pīṭhāni catvāri  pīṭhadevyāścatuṣṭayam 
ādyaṃ varṇaṃ catunyāsa napuṃsakatrikaṃ tathā 
caturdīrghasamākrāntā khaśaktyā śekharāṅkitāḥ 
u ū śūnyakalā candra śivabīja caturvidham 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
taccaika sarvato deva dvitīyaṃ dviguṇīkṛtam 
tṛtīyaṃ tu tridhā sthāpya caturthaṃ ca caturguṇam 
pañcamaṃ pañcaguṇitametad vai kulapañcakam 
pañcajo bhrajamāno'sau prasāda śivamakṣaram 
śambhuśakterbhavet ṣaṭkaṃ vidyāṣaṭka yathā bhavet 
haraīṣaṭkaṣaṭka ca kṣobhakena kṛtaṃ śiram 
phara  e  meti candrāka dvāvetau ṣaḍvidhā kuru 
teṣāmante sthitā ṣaḍbhi dīrghabinduśikhānvitā 
M
akṣarā ṣaḍibhirvidyā svayambhoḥ ṣaṭkamityapi 
vyomapañcakanāmāni' idānīṃ vyāptipañcakam  
pṛthivyādi tridhā sthāpya īśvareṇa vibheditam 
āptattva triguṇīṭya  dīrghatrayavibheditāḥ 
caturthaṃ vāyutattva tu ratnatritayabheditam 
pañcamaṃ vyomatattva tu trikalāṅkitabheditam 
tridhāste  vyāpakāḥ pañca bindunādapadāṅkitāḥ 
tadādau bindutattvaṃ tu pṛthivyāsanameva ca 
ā  ī  u kārabhinnāste khacandraśikharāṅkitāḥ 
evaṃ te trīṇi siddhāstu saṃsthitā jñānarūpataḥ 
yathākrameṇa vṛddhasya mantrakrama samuddhṛtam 
vidhānaṃ ca mahādeva yathā kaumāravṛddhakam 
tathā saṃketabhāṣā ca nāmasaṃketasūcanam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
ojāpūkāñca catvāra  kāpūjāocatuṣṭayam 
mā vi sajja samu ceti saṃketakamida punaḥ 
ete guptatarā pīṭhā guptāśca pīṭhadevatāḥ 
pīṭhasiddhāśca catvāraḥ saṃketa susūkṣmakam 
kulapañcakamanya tu tasya saṃketa pañcadhā 
aku saku sakuśceti aṃku caiva aku punaḥ 
kulapañcakametad hi ambhāṣaṭkamataḥ param 
aṃbhā ca ṣaḍvidhāṃ kuryāt catuḥsvaravibheditām  
tasyāgre cādhikārāṇi vṛddhadevyāḥ ṣaḍirbhavet 
āpa iti ma aṃkāra ma avvā krama tathā 
ma
kha a ced  bhakārāvvā ambhāṣaṭkamiti
etad vai kaulabhāṣāyāṃ mantrakramamudāhṛtam 
yogapañcakameva tu tasya saṃketa pañcadhā 
asā sasa vayogeti saku 
īsasaka iti 
guptaṃ prakaṭasaṃyogāt pūrvakramasamāyutam 
siddhatrikaṃ trikasyaiva teṣu saṃketa tridhā 
si siddha iti siddhāstu sarve mantrakramoditāḥ 
kṛtvā pūrvakramācāra prakārāṇi samabhyaset 
upadeśavaśenaiva kaumārakramamuddhṛtam 
adhunā madhyamolyāyā krameda caiva ṣaḍvidham 
smṛtam 
catuṣkaṃ pañcakaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ catuṣkaṃ pañcakaṃ trikam 
etāni ṣaṭprakārāṇi bhedāni saptaviṃśatiḥ 
ādau pīṭhacatuṣkaṃ tu catvāraḥ pīṭhadevatāḥ
pūrṇagirya samārabhya udaya madhyamolike
aparaṃ ca pravakṣyāmi bālakramamanuttamam 
pūrvakrameṇa vakṣyāmi mudrāpīṭhāditaḥ
kramāt 
pīṭhānāmādyaliṅgāni catūratnasamāyutāḥ
ātmākūṭā kṛtāḥ sarve paścāt pīṭhacatuṣṭayam
mantradevya punasteṣāṃ catvāraḥ sāmprataṃ bhavet 
prathamaṃ vāgbhavaṃ bījaṃ māyābījaṃ dvitīyakam 
tṛtīyaṃ sūryabījaṃ tu khecaraṃ tu caturthakam 
vidyātmāna mahākūṭaṃ eka deva caturvidham 
pañcamaṃ navadhā piṇḍaṃ śukrādīnā bhaved yathā 
śaktyākāśāntajaṃ rudra indurānandabodhakam 
taraṅga śaktipātaṃ tu navātmānandavigraham 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
khaśaktimastakākrāntaṃ ākrānta nādamūrdhani 
śaktyāveśaṃ tu dhāraṇā 
ojāpūkeṣu cetyādau
ādināthakramākhyāta
pañcamaṃ siddhanāyakam 
śrīnāthaṃ śrīguru mūlaṃ ājñāsantatinirṇayam 
sarva krameṣu sādhāraṃ ādhāramiti bhairavam 
tasyoccāraṇamātreṇa sarvāvastho bhaviṣyati 
siddhapañcakameva tu catuḥpīṭheṣu saṃsthitam 
pañcamaṃ yat paraṃ nāthaṃ śrīguru madhyanāyakam 
siddhau dvāviti vikhyātī ādyapīṭhasya suvrata 
aparaṃ jñānaṣaṭkaṃ tu vakṣye kaulasya nāyakam 
vidyāyā kāraṇaṃ cātra tacca eva caturvidham 
sahajaṃ māyayārūḍhaṃ ānandakulabheditam 
ma  ekhapharapiṇḍastha vāgbhavasthaṃ maheśvara 
turyatoraṇaśaktyo vyāpakaṃ kulayoginām kumārikākhaṇḍa
tat sa binduradho daṇḍaṃ anilārṇavapūritam 
ghaṇṭānirghoṣasahitaṃ aṃguṣṭhena śirāhatam 
haṃsavarṇodaye siddhaṃ dvinapuṃsakaditam 
ākrāntaṃ nādavarṇābhyāṃ tathānyaṃ vyāpakaṃ bhavet 
catvāro vyāpakākāśe tadadhaḥ śaktibimbakam 
visargastha mahādevyā vyāpaka sarvatomukham 
sṛṣṭikrameṇa mūrdhādi ājñācakrādivigraha sudhīḥ 
jñānaṣaṭkamidaṃ tathyaṃ devānāmapi durlabham 
aparaṃ ca mahantāyīḥ pañcakaṃ sāmprataṃ viduḥ 
tṛtīyasya tu vargasya dvitīyavarṇanāyakam 
kartavyaṃ pañcaguṇitaṃ dīrghapañcakabheditam 
ājñāmaṇḍalamadhyastha  trirāvarta maheśvaram 
sa caika kevalaṃ bhūyasteṣāṃ cādisthitaṃ kuru 
olitritayasiddhāśca trikaṃ teṣāṃ yathā bhavet 
anunāsika catvāri adho bandukṛtāni vai 
ekībhūtaṃ mahākūṭa yojayet trividhaṃ punaḥ 
ūkāraṃ caiva īkāra ākārādi vibhedayet 
nādaśaktikalābhinnaṃ
jyeṣṭhamadhyamaka nyaset 
tribhirolīṣu te deva mantracakraṃ tridhoddhṛtam 
etanmantrakrama cakraṃ saṃketaṃ tasya gīyate 
devīnāmādyavarṇena guptaṃ pīṭhacatuṣṭayam
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tathā tenaiva pīṭhānāṃ jñeyaṃ devyācatuṣṭayam 
aṃkunātha ca ciṃ caiva kakārākṣarasaṃjñayā 
evaṃ siddhaṃ catuṣkaṃ tu yugmasaṃjñā tu pañcakam 
śikhāśekharamākrāntaṃ ku  i avasamāyutam 
siddhapañcakametaddhi pīṭheṣu ca samārabhet 
jñānaṣaṭkasya saṃketa idamākarṇatā prabho 
ākhe iti visañcaiva avidyā ca tathā param 
mama ceti tathā svāsū āmei jñānaṣaṭkakam 
aparaṃ ca mahantāyī pañcakasya ca sūcanam 
avimā hyekato vyāpti samu ceti ca yo mukha 
sa ca anyakrameṇaiva samasteṣviti pañcakam 
evaṃ te ṣaṭkārāṇi bhedāni saptaviṃśatiḥ
ādau pīṭhacatuṣkaṃ tu catvāraḥ pīṭhadevatāḥ 
siddhapañcakamanya tu jñānaṣaṭkaṃ tathāparam 
mahantāryāī pañcakaṃ ca olitrikamanantaram 
etad bālakramākhyātaṃ pañcapraṇavabheditam 
lakṣāśramapadasaṃyukta  vṛddhakaumāraka smṛtam 
ākhyātā ca kaniṣṭholi kāmarūpāditaḥ kramāt 
jyeṣṭhaṃ madhyamasaṃjñaṃ ca tathā bālaṃ tṛtīyakam 
ākhyātaṃ paścimāmnāye kramamekaṃ tridhāvidham 
olibhedena kartavyaṃ svaolyā kramapūjanam 
svaoli maṇḍalaṃ cakraṃ krama mantropadeśakam 
pāramparyamukhāmnāyaṃ siddhasantānasantatau 
bhāṣāsaṃketaka  sūtraṃ jñātvā ājñā pravartate kumārikākhaṇḍa
paścāt kulakrama pūjyaṃ anyathā na kadācana 
oliranyā kriyā cānyā anya mantraparigraham 
pūjāvidhānamanyaṃ tu maṇḍalaṃ vyutkrameṇa tu 
vṛddhakaumārabāla  vā anyaṃ vā khecarakramam 
aśuddhaṃ śrīkramaṃ yasmādabhyasto'pi na siddhyati 
siddhayate vā pramādena guruvaktrād vinirgatam 
ante vighnapradaṃ śiṣye aśuddhaṃ caiva śodhayet 
aśuddhaṃ pūjayed yastu dadyād yaḥ śāstralopakṛt 
sa tasya hanate nūnaṃ śiṣyamācāryastatkṣaṇāt 
śiṣyasya grahaṇāt mṛtyuracirādapi  nānyathā 
sadbhaktasya svaśiṣyasya śāstralopa na kārayet 
abhakte ca śaṭhe deva kriyālopakare tathā 
na tasya dāpayed jñānaṃ kramaṃ maṇḍalakādikam 
tathā kulāgatāṃ cājñāṃ  upadeśaṃ ca gopayet 
bhayāt prītyārthalobhād vā mahatvapadakāṃkṣayā
yo dadet kramamoghānāṃ sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam 
aviyogācca maraṇaṃ saṃskāra naivamarhati 
krama vidyāmaṃ yo gopanī prayatnataḥ 
sarvasvaṃ rakṣayet jñānaṃ caurebhyo draviṇaṃ yathā 
pañcopacārapūjāyāṃ arcayitvā kulāgamam 
ādyogha cintayed buddhyā antaraṅgena suvrata 
bahiraṅgaṃ yadā kuryād darśayeditare jane
ājñābhaṅga na saṃdeha khyāpanānnarake gatiḥ 
karmaṇā manasā vācā triśuddhirbhaktivatsala 
sadbhaktasya vinītasya dvādaśābdaparīkṣite  
anugraha prakartavyaṃ śāstraṃ tasyāvatārayet kumārikākhaṇḍa
anyathā naiva kartavyaṃ jihvopasthanimittaye 
jihvopasthanimittaye śrīkramaṃ pravadanti ye
kathayanti mukhāmnāyaṃ ājñāśāstramidaṃ kulam 
na teṣāmaihikī siddhiḥ paratra ca na vidyate 
akramāllobhamohād vā mithyāhaṃkāragarvitaḥ 
akramād gṛhyate śāstraṃ āmnāyaṃ mukhakaulikam 
tat tasya niṣphalaṃ sarva ākāśe kumudaṃ yathā 
tathā ca niṣphalā ceṣṭā akramācaraṇād bhavet 
kramapūjāratā  śāntā rāgadveṣavivarjitāḥ 
te ca yogyā kule kaule śeṣāstvantarajātayaḥ 
lobhād yo gṛhaṇate śāstraṃ aihikārthaṃ ca sundara 
kītyarthaṃ ca yaśārtha vā putrakasya kṛte'thavā 
mantrī kramapadasyārthe adhikāra prayacchati 
sa tasya hanate deva mahādroho na saṃśayaḥ 
viṣṭhāmadhye kṛmirbhūtvā amedhye sūpajīvati 
pratyuttāra na vidyeta tadvat tasyādhamā gatiḥ 
kramaṃ ca trividhaṃ proktaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tathā param 
śākta ca śāmbhava caiva āṇava ca tṛtīyakam 
parāpara ca aparaṃ paraṃ ceti trikaṇṭakam 
ekaṃ tritrikabhedena tridhā olikramaṃ viduḥ 
sthūlaṃ vṛddhakramākhyātaṃ jyeṣṭha  olyādhikārakam 
sūkṣmakramaṃ ca kaumāraṃ susūkṣmamiti gīyate 
paraṃ bālakrama bhāvya  kaniṣṭholitṛtīyakam 
eka  eva  tridhā bhinnaṃ kramameka trikaṇṭakam 
śrīkramaṃ tu tridhā prokta tridhā olikramaṃ viduḥ kumārikākhaṇḍa
mama dehād viniṣkrāntā kramāścatvāri sundara 
khecara ca kramaṃ cādyaṃ vṛddhakaumārabālakam 
teṣāṃ caturyugā siddhiḥ sva  olyānukrama tathā 
kṛte tu khecaraṃ prokta tretā vṛddhakramaṃ tathā  
dvāpare kramakaumāra kalau bālakrama kramam 
evaṃ te kramacatvāra  yugānte cāvatāritāḥ 
kalau yuge mahādeva krama jñeyaṃ caturvidham 
teṣāṃ ca udaya  vakṣye tathā cāstamana punaḥ 
udayāstamanenaiva jñeyaṃ kramacatuṣṭayam 
mama dehād viniṣkrāntā vidhānaṃ teṣu tacchṛṇu 
anāmānāmasaṃlagnā tanmadhye khecara kramam  
nirgataṃ jñānasāmathyānmajjamadhye layaṃgatam 
aparaṃ yat kramaṃ vṛddhaṃ mama krodhād vinirgatam 
snāyorantargata deva etaccāstamanaṃ smṛtam 
kaumāraṃ nābhicakrasthaṃ tasmāt sthānād vinirgatam 
laya ca śoṇite tasya udayāstamana  tvidam 
tathā bālakrama nāma yonicakrād vinirgatam 
vilīnaṃ śukramadhye tu udayāstamanatrayam kumārikākhaṇḍa
kramatrayasamāyukta udayāstamanasaṃyutam 
sa śiṣya paścimāmnāye śeṣā'nye nāmadhārakāḥ 
śṛṇu nātha pravakṣyāmi kramamekaṃ tridhā yathā 
yasmin kāle layaṃ sarva mama dehe prajāyante 
na candrārkagrahā ṛkṣā na loko naiva parvataḥ 
na
nāhaṃ deva na ca tvaṃ vā śūnyaṃ bhūtaṃ carācaram 
tasmāccaiva nirākārād divyājñāyāḥ samudbhavaḥ 
śivecchā nirgatā śaktiraṃkurākārarūpiṇī 
taḍillatā  samākārā dyotayantī nabhastalam 
tena cīrṇaṃ tapa cogra divyājñāyā jitendriyam 
tataḥ sā unmanā jātā vṛddhatvaṃ samupāgatā 
aṃkuraṃ tu dvidhābhinnaṃ sākāra  tu nirañjanam 
śivaśaktisamāyoga gīyate sarvajantuṣu 
tvaṃ śivo deva kaulīśa ahaṃ sā kubjinī parā 
mama rūpatrayo jāta khecarakāraṇena tu 
pratyūṣe bālarūpāhaṃ yuvāhaṃ dinamadhyataḥ 
niśācāreṇa vṛddhāhaṃ mama eṣā tridhā gatiḥ 
tasmāt tu trividhaṃ prokta kramamekaṃ kulakrame 
bālakrame ca bālāvvā tadā bālakramaṃ bhavet 
madhyāhne yuvakaumāraṃ tenāsau madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ 
vṛddhaṃ tu vṛddharūpī syāt sandhyākālasamarpitam 
tribhirmūrtivaśenaiva kramameka tridhā bhavet 
teṣu vidyā hyahaṃ devyā ṣaḍvaktrāṅgasamanvitā 
tathā kulāṣṭakaṃ bāhye kramamaṇḍalaveṣṭitam 
kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
maṇḍitaṃ yaistu trailokya nānārūpaṃ nabhākṛti 
tena te maṇḍalā proktā udyāstamanavarjitāḥ'
maṇḍalā dyotagā sarve tridhā baddhamaśeṣata
kramodayamidaṃ hyetat tridhā baddhamaśeṣataḥ 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kuladevyāṣṭakaṃ yathā 
aṣṭavargākṣarānyaṣṭau aiṃkārāntavibheditā 
nādabindusamākrāntā nābhisthā kuladevatā 
bījatrayaṃ tu prāsādaṃ rāvabījaṃ tu pañcamam 
aṣṭāvante samāsṛjyā vargadevyastvanantaram 
brāhmī māheśa kaumārī vaiṣṇavī ca varāhikā 
indrāṇī caiva āgneyī cāmuṇḍā ceti cāṣṭamī 
navamī ca mahālakṣmī savisargapradīpitā 
pañcapraṇavāditaḥ kṛtvā saṃyogānnavakaṃ prati  
vicceti pādukāntaṃ tu kṛtvā yajanamārabhet 
olīnāmetat samaya samayāyuktavidyayā 
kramasyāvaraṇa proktaṃ jñātvā siddhyāriho bhavet 
saptāviṃśatibhedāni  trividhena krameṇa tu 
uktā ye ca mayā deva teṣāṃ saṃketakāni me 
pādukānāṃ ca pīṭhānā siddhanāthakrameṇa tu 
devatā ye krame sarve avvāśabda niyojayet 
pādukāntaṃ tathāgre tu kramaṃ pūjya yathāvidhiḥ' 
eteṣā ca kramāṇāṃ ca udayāstamana punaḥ 
ādyakramasya deveśa udaya cādyapīṭhake 
layaṃ vai tisrapīṭhe tu ādyasya khecarasya
kumārikākhaṇḍa
tathā vṛddhakramasyaiva udayaṃ tisrapīṭhakeṃ  
kāmarūpe layaṃ tasya kaumārasya tathā punaḥ 
udayaṃ pūrṇagiryāyāṃ layaṃ tasyādyapīṭhake 
tathā bālakramasyaiva udayaṃ kāmarūpake 
layamoṃkārapīṭhe tu etat kramavinirṇayam 
ākhyātaṃ pūrvasūtre'smin jñātvā cānvayiko bhavet 
kramapūrve samāpte tu ājñāsūtraṃ tu yoginaḥ 
sakṛdāvartanāt tasyā ājñāsiddhirmalakṣayam 
ityādyāvatāre mahāmanthānabhairavayajñe anvaye saptakoṭipramāṇe merumārgavinirgate
lakṣapādādhike ādyapīṭhāvatārite vidyāpīṭhamārge vimalaṣaṭkanirṇaye 
kādibhede ājñāpārameśvare svāminīmate śrīcaturviṃśatsahasrasahitāyā
avvākramabhāṣite kramatridhādhikāravarṇane
kramodayo nāmānandaḥ  
ūnatriṃśānandaḥ
śrīnātha uvāca
ahaṃ śiṣya  svarūpeṇa kṛpāṃ 'me kuru kaulini' 
yat kiñcidājñayā devi prasādaṃ kriyatāṃ prabho 
anādinidhane' śānte ādināthe kulodbhave 
kandaguhyāntarāvasthe' namāmi paramāmṛte 
dvādaśānte trikoṇasthe kandādhārasamudbhave 
vāme vāmāntarālīne namāmi paramāvyaye 
sarvakāmaiḥ susaṃpūrṇe icchāśaktiradhiṣṭhite 
icchayā sṛjaseṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  
kāmeśvarīti kāmākhye kāmarūpe svayaṃbhuve 
kāmapīṭhāntarāvasthe kāmarūpe namāmi te 
bindumadhyād viniṣkrānte kāmeśvari bhagālaye 
guptakāmākhyaguhyānte mahāsiddhairalaṃkṛte 
sarvaratneṣu khacite mahāmaṇivibhūṣite 
muktāphalapravālādyairbhūṣite sumanorame 
vajravaiḍūryaracite indranīlairvicitrite 
anekaratnasaṃdīpte mahāratnavibhūṣite 
sugandhagandhabahule kuṃkumodakacarcite 
karpūrādibhirdhūpaiśca madirānandanandite 
sugandhāmodabahule pañcakādye manohare 
nānākusumajātībhirnānāvarṇairadhiṣṭhite 
pūjyase siddhavṛndaiśca' candratārāgaṇāvṛte 
khecarīcakramadhyasthe mandarasthe napuṃsake 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
pañcāśalliṅgajanani yonirūpe mahāmbike 
guhyāntāvasthite devi guhāgahanavāsini 
na strī na ca puliṅga ānanda tannapuṃsakam 
ratnaikādaśasaṃsthāne tvaṃ hi devi virājase 
khyātu tvāṃ naiva śaknomi saṃkṣepeṇoditaṃ mayā 
mahāratnastava guhyaṃ divyānandapravartakam 
stutiṃ kṛtvā tu pṛcchāmi kāmarūpe śṛṇu priye 
kaścāhaṃ tvaṃ ca kā devi kiṃ nāma iha gīyate 
na jānāmi svarūpaṃ te tejaśaktyā  prabhāvataḥ 
praṇāma varṇarūpaṃ vā pāramparyavyavasthitam 
pīṭhaṃ mantropadeśañca kramācāra yathā sthitam 
mama līnā sadā magnā nāhaṃ jānāmi te padam 
devadevapriye devi mama prāṇeṣu vallabhe 
na tvayā rahitaṃ kiñcit paśyāmi sacarācare 
prasādaṃ kuru me gauri bhaktasya mā sulocane 
kiñcid rahasyaṃ deveśi kaulajñāna sudurlabham 
yasyāvatāramātreṇa siddhirbhavati kalau yuge 
tadahaṃ śrotumicchāmi nisaṃśaya vadasva me 
śrīvakrā uvāca 
śṛṇu īśvara tattvena kāraṇaṃ gūḍhamuttamam 
guhyād guhyataraṃ guhyaṃ gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ 
yoginīhṛdayaṃ guhyaṃ atiguhya surakṣitam 
rakṣaṇīya sadā śambho caurebhyo draviṇaṃ yathā kumārikākhaṇḍa
paratejād viniṣkrāntā avyaktā vyaktarūpiṇī 
dakṣabhāge sthitaḥ śambhuḥ vāme viṣṇuḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
madhyavartī sthito brahmā bindurūpī mahābalaḥ 
tanmadhyavartinī cāhaṃ tejorūpeṇa saṃsthitā 
bhūrbhuva svādilokeṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca 
nakṣatragraharāśīṣu kṛmikīṭādiṣu sthitā 
mātṛkāvarṇarūpā ca mama yonyāntare sthitā 
pīṭhopapīṭhakṣetrāṇi catvārāṇi tathā pare 
yoginīsiddhanilaya yat kiñcid vāṅmayaṃ sthitam 
sṛjāmi sakalaṃ viśvaṃ saṃhāriṣyāmyaha punaḥ 
guhye hṛdi tathā vaktre sthitāhaṃ paramā kalā 
sthūlasūkṣmavibhāgena śṛṇu mūrti yathā sthitām 
tā te'ha saṃpravakṣyāmi divyarūpāṃ mahābalām 
ekākṣarā parā proktā siddhānāṃ jñānabhūmikā 
yogavidyā mahāvidyā rudrāṇāṃ hṛdaye sthitā 
rudrakhaṇḍe tu rudrāṇāṃ parā jñānānuvartinī 
kāmākhye samayā proktā pīṭhadevī ca pūrṇake 
yogisaṃjñā ca oṃkāre mudrātritayamaṇḍale 
vidyātritayasaṃyukta avatāra yuge yuge 
olīnā gotravarge'smin amaryādiṣu śāsa 
parā ekākṣarā pūrva tava deva nidarśitā 
tā pravakṣyāmyaha samyak susūkṣmā lakṣamadhyagām  
kumārikākhaṇḍa
ādau hrasvasvarā proktā unnatā kiñcid dṛśyate 
nīlotpaladalaśyāmā vīrabhasmasamaprabhā
ṣaḍvaktrā ṣaṭkārā ca cicchaktyantaracāriṇī 
netrairaṣṭādaśaiścaiva vartulścāvalokinī 
dvādaśaiśca bhujairyuktā nānāsragdāmamaṇḍitā 
pretasiṃhāsanāsīnā nānābharaṇaśobhitā
kulakoṭisahasrāṇā ārūḍhā kulaśāsane 
tasyāḥ piṇḍavidhānokta devānāmapi durlabham 
ananta pādayornitya nupūraparimaṇḍaṇam 
takṣakaṃ kaṭibandhe tu mekhalāyā virājate
karkoṭaka karṇau devyāḥ kaṇṭhe vāsukibhairavam 
mukuṭe kulikaṃ caiva gonāsa karṇakuṇḍale 
kharjuramudrikāṃgulyairanye nāgakulāni ca 
bhrūdaṇḍe saṃsthitaḥ padmo mahāpadmo dvitīyakeṃ 
khaṭvāṅga pāśamabhaya akṣasūtraṃ suśobhanam 
mañjarīṃ ratnakhacita vidyutpuñjasamadyutim 
koṭyāgamakareṇaiva śaṅkhapālastathottare 
kapāla varada caiva triśūlaṃ karmadarpaṇam 
dakṣiṇe ca kare devyā amarīdravyapañcakam 
kalaśaṃ dvānavatyāyāḥ śatairdvibhiḥ virājate 
svaramālā śire devyā varṇahārāvalambinī 
vṛścikairgalake hāra śatārthena virājate 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
parādevīmukhaṃ pūrva ūdhvastha rājate śubham 
gokṣīradhavala divya  kalāsaptādaśīyutam 
dvitīya mūrdhni vaktra tu gagana nāma mālinī 
śaṅkhendutuhinābhāsaṃ saumyamūrtiḥ suśobhanam 
tṛtīyaṃ pūrvavaktraṃ tu pāṇḍura krodhavihvalam 
siddhayogeśvarīkhyāta mantravigrahabhūṣitam 
nīlotpalanibhaprakhyaṃ kālikākhyaṃ tu dakṣiṇe 
daṃṣṭra karāla raudraṃ ca kiñcidraktāyatekṣaṇam 
dāḍimīkusumaprakhyaṃ saumyamānandadāyakam 
pañcamaṃ tripurā nāma pūrṇacandreva vartulam 
umākhecaripūrvaṃ tu paścima  śvetarūpakam 
sarvānugrahakṛd divyaṃ dhyātaṃ mokṣaphalapradam 
svacchadarpaṇasaṃkāśa hṛdayaṃ tu virājate 
bālārkakiraṇaprakhyaṃ śirasa tejavarcasam 
taḍitkoṭisahasrābhā śikhā bhāsvararūpiṇī 
kavacaṃ tejadurbhedya duṣprekṣya bahurūpiṇam 
netrau candrārkatulyābhau tṛtīyaṃ vahnisannibham 
astraṃ kālānalacchāyaṃ lelihānaṃ suduḥsaham 
sarva saṃhārayet tveva tejasā paribhāvayet 
pṛthivī jānudeśe tu apo nābhyāṃ vyavasthitaḥ 
tejo hṛdayamadhye tu kaṇṭhasthāne tu mārutam ir
ākāśaṃ tu lalāṭastha brahmā
nābhigata  viduḥ  
kumārikākhaṇḍa
hṛdi madhye sthito viṣṇuḥ kaṇṭhasthaṃ rudrasaṃjñakam 
īśvara tu lalāṭasthaṃ tadūve śivamavyayam 
sarvavyāptisvarūpeṇa viśvarūpā yaśasvinī 
agnivāsaparīdhānā tejapuñjasamaprabhā 
dhyāyed devyāstvidaṃ rūpaṃ āpūryantaṃ vicintayet 
eṣā sā unmanā sūkṣmā sā kalā bhuvanāntare 
uditā kalikāle tu devadevī jagatsutā 
ākāśe martyaloke ca pātāle hāṭṭakere 
sasthitā olivarge tu ājñārūpā ca koṅkaṇe 
devyā mūrtimimāṃ śambho jñātvā yajanamārabhet

śrīvakrā uvāca'
likhyamāne mahādeva cāturviṃśasahasra 
śrīmate matarājāne khaṇḍatrayamahākule 
vidhihīnasya vighnāni jāyante ca yathā śṛṇu 
utpātā  saṃprajāyante vighnāni ca anekadhā 
vyādhayaśca prakupyante rājānaḥ svajane api 
svagṛhe kalaho nityaṃ udvegaścātidāruṇa 
sagotrāñca prakupyante kalahaṃ ca parasparam
arthahāniralābhaśca viyogaśca suhṛdbadhaḥ 
kapotāśca gṛhe nityaṃ āruhanti viśanti
gṛdrāḥ kākāñca kākolā paryaṭanti
pariveśa tu sūryasya akāle kuhuka
garbhan sravanti garbhiṇyo garjana
ulkāpātā diśo dāgho pārravataścāgnidīpanam 
rātrau svapnāni raudrāṇi paśyate satataṃ priya 
candrasvātiprakopena vātā vāyanti bhīṣaṇāḥ 
praviśanti gṛhasyānte vyālāścātiviṣotkaṭāḥ 
paṭhedanādarād yastu jāyate tasya tadṛśam

cāpi jāyate kumārikākhaṇḍa
rakṣanti siddhayoginyaḥ siddhāśca daṇḍadhārakāḥ 
koṭikoṭistvasaṃkhyātā śrīmateda mahākulam 
adṛṣṭavigrahā nityaṃ yogasiddhā mahābalāḥ 
rakṣanti śrīmata deva śāsane kulayoginaḥ 
daśadikṣu pravartante śivārāvā bhayaṃkarā  
piṅgalāśca gṛhe nityaṃ śabdaṃ kurvanti dāruṇam 
gṛdhracitā varāroha viśanti tasya mandire 
evamādi  mahotpātā vidhihīnasya niścitam 
samayaghnasya viśeṣeṇa vighnasaṃkhyā na vidyate 
tadarthastu vidhiḥ kāryo likhyamāne ca pratyayam  
saṃvidhāsyāmi te deva sarvavighnavināśanam 
yatnato pustaka rakṣya saṃsparśāt taddbahiḥ kṛtaiḥ 
yatnena tu vidhiḥ kāryo yāvad granthaḥ samāpyate 
tatsaṃsthānavihīnatvāt spaṣṭa naiva prajāyate 
tithiṃ pūrṇa samāsādya sūryeṇa tu samanvitām
guruvāre'thavā deva duṣṭa  ṛkṣa vivarjayet 
aṣṭamyā vā caturdaśyā śubha  ṛkṣaṇayogataḥ 
ekānte vijane ramye paśudṛṣṭivivarjite 
gomayenopalipte ca nimnonnatavivarjite 
kṛtvā maṇḍalakaṃ tatra caturastraṃ samantataḥ 
puṣpaprakarasaṃkīrṇe svastikopari śobhite 
vidikṣu dīpakāstatra dātavyā ghṛtabodhitāḥ 
svastikopari saṃsthāpya kumbhaṃ cāliprapūritam 
pūjayet tu trikhaṇḍaṃ vai puṣpamālāvibhūṣitam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
āsane tu trikhaṇḍaṃ tu khaṇḍa vai mātṛkhaṇḍakam 
mantrakhaṇḍaṃ tu vai madhye navātmānena pūritam 
tatra pustakamāropya likhitaṃ vā alekhitam 
veṣṭayed vastrayugmena hemagarbha tu kārayet 
pūjyaṃ pañcopacāreṇa naivedyaṃ vinivedayet 
bahirbaliḥ pradātavyo ācāryeṇa vidhānavat 
tato maṅgalanirghoṣairlekhayet ślokapañcakam  
saṃvatīmaṇḍalaṃ sūtra avatāraṃ kramasya tu 
vyākhyeya lekhayet kvāpi yathāvidhiranukramāt 
samayīsādhakān putrān yoginyaśca kumārikāḥ 
ārātrī pūrvata kārya alipātrāṇi pūrayet 
śirasā kulakumbhaṃ tu natvā caiva tataḥ punaḥ 
kumāryāhvānayeccāṣṭauṃ gandha' dhūpa pradāpayet 
yogīśvarān samīpasthān yogina kuladīkṣitān 
pūjayet kusumaiḥ śreṣṭhaiḥ śreṣṭhadhūpena dhūpayet 
saṃtapya alinā sarvaṃ matsyamāṃsāni dāpayet 
tadante prārthayeccājñā bhagavatyāḥ kuladīkṣitān 
śrīmataṃ tu likhiṣyāmi avighnena prasiddhyatu 
labdhvānujñastu yogīndraḥ pūjayitvā kulakramamṃ 
saṃpūjya pustakaṃ tatra vidhinā ca prayatnataḥ 
dehasthā devatāḥ sarvāḥ tarpayed bhaktitatparaḥ 
khjña
tato maṅgalanirghoṣaiḥ śaṃkhavāditraniḥsvanaiḥ 
divyāṅganāsugītaiśca saṃvatīmaṇḍalaṃ likhet 
lekhakañca tataḥ pūjya sragavastrāsavādikaiḥ  
māṅgalyaistūryanirghoṣaiḥ stotravīṇāmahāsvanaiḥ 
prathame'hani deveśa kuryāccakraprapūjanam 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
cakrakrīḍā samāśritya tuhina kṣepayet sudhīḥ 
evaṃ tu prathame dine pratyahaṃ śaktitaḥ punaḥ 
kriyate ca vidhiprājñaiḥ bali  rātrau dine dine 
yāvat samāpyate grantha tāvat kuryād vidhi
anyathā prāpnuyācchāpas mahāntaṃ yoginīkulāt 
tadartha bhaktinā lekhya anyathā vighnadāyakam 
tvimām 
iti evaṃvidhaṃ deva śrīmateda mahākulam 
nāpuṇyoṃ labhate mayo yoginīgarbhavarjitaḥ 
idaṃ guhyaṃ ca sarvasvaṃ cāturviṃśatsahasrakam 
naiva deyamabhaktānāṃ na śaṭhān krūrakarmiṇām 
tāntrikānā na dātavyaṃ tārkikāṇā viśeṣataḥ 
na dāmbhikāya mūkhīya na deyaṃ klīvakrodhine  
nāhaṃkṛte ca pāpiṣṭe cchadmake copajīvake 
svargapātālikā bhogā yena tyaktā hi sundara 
saṃsārabhayabhītātmā gurusmaraṇamāśritaḥ 
deya gurvānvite śiṣye abhakte ca na dāpayet 
gurubhaktāya śāntāya samayācāranispṛhe 
gūḍhajñānasuśāntāya satyavādījitendriye 
ihajanmāvadhiryena saṃnyasta gurūṇāṃ prati 
manovākkāyakarmaṇā guroricchānuvartinaḥ 
tasya deyamidaṃ guhyaṃ dvādaśābdaparīkṣite
saṃketa yo vijānāti  tathā sāṃvatsaraṃ kramam 
mūlasūtraṃ kramaṃ deyaṃ pāramparyagurukramam 
tathā vai ṣoḍaśaḥ parva sūcitāste mahītale 
saṃpradāyavaśenaiva tasya deyaṃ kulāgamam 
nābhivartirahīkā ca vajrasandhi kapāṭayoḥ 
saṃketān vetti yo'pyatra tasya deyaṃ kulāgamam 
śrīnātha uvāca
tava śiṣyo'haṃ prītaḥ siddho'habhairavo haraḥ
kṛtamantrādhikārī ca adyāhaṃ kulanāyike 
kulakramaṃ ca kaulaṃ ca upadeśaḥ kathaṃ kriyā 
brūhi jñānaṃ surendrākhye vakrāmnāyaḥ kathaṃ kulam

kumārikākhaṇḍa
nābhivartirahistākṣyo vidyā vajraḥ kapāṭayoḥ
jñānamaṣṭaprakāro'yaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ paścimānvayam 
yo jānāti varāroha sa bhavenmatabodhaka 
śrīnātha uvāca
kā nābhivartikā devi ahivṛkṣaśca ko punaḥ 
kā vidyā kaśca vajrākhyaḥ kapāṭau ca kathaṃ vada 
mūlaṃ nābhi kulaṃ merurvartirātmā ca mālinī 
pāramparyamahijñāna sandhirājñākramodayam 
vṛkṣaṃ vajrakula' dvīpaṃ ṣaṭkoṇākhyaṃ kapāṭayoḥ 
etad dīpanavijñāna kādibhede udāhṛtam 
punaranya tu bhedena śṛṇu bhairava tattvataḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
nābhirmerukrama kīrti bhedājñā saptaviṃśatiḥ 
ṣaṭ padāḥ ṣaḍi mudrāśca caturādau catuḥ punaḥ 
pañcakaṃ ca tathā ṣaṭkaṃ punaḥ pañcātmakaṃ catuḥ 
evaṃ kramodaya yat tat karṇāt karṇopadeśakam 
pūjākramavidhāna tu nābhijñānaṃ kulakramam 
tasya vartistrikoṇe tu triṣkoṇā śaktiravyayā 
sā bhūmiḥ sthitiviśrāmaṃ tasyāmnāya mukhāgamam 
ahirākāśamudadhi  saṃvartamiti maṇḍalam 
sadyāveśakramāruhya vāmāvartaparibhramāt 
vāyumaṇḍalamākhyātaṃ turyasthamahisaṃjñayā
tatra lakṣaṃ vinikṣipya bhūmikā grāhya vaiṣṇavīm
sā kalā dravate tatra golakāmṛtacandrikā 
etat samādhikaraṇa yoginīnāṃ prapadyate 
jñātvācāragatiṃ rudra ahiśabdaṃ samabhyaset 
tāraṇād gurutākṣyañca vidyārājaṃ navātmakam 
sa eva bhairavo'nantaḥ śukrādiḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
tākṣya evaṃ samākhyātaṃ gurūṇāṃ paramo guruḥ 
bhakārādicakārāntā vidyārājñī śivānanā 
gurorutsaṅgagā vidyā pañcānte pañcamūrdhani 
vidyā candrakalā jyotsnā mahantāyī prakīrtitā 
anayā bhāvitātmā tu sa cātmā navadhā smṛtaḥ 
kumārikākhaṇḍa
vidyopadeśamākhyātaṃ devānāmapi durlabham 
vajrātmanaḥ smṛtaṃ piṇḍaṃ vajrapiṇḍa ca ṣaḍvidham 
kulaṃ tat ṣaṭprakāraṃ tu uktaṃ vai sarvadehinām 
ādhārādibhruvorantaṃ ṣaṭprakāramahārṇavam 
vajrasaṃketamākhyātaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā 
ca vṛkṣaṃ svakaṃ piṇḍaṃ vṛkṣasya bāhyataḥ kramam 
tasyodayaṃ ca vilayaṃ śivaśaktigamāgamam 
śaktirmūla  kalāpūrṇa saṃpūrṇamiti pūraka 
tasyodhve śvasano yastu saṃhāra iti recakaḥ 
sa śiva kulavṛkṣasya pralayodayakāraka  
dvāvimau ca kapāṭākhyauprāṇāpānasvarūpakau 
evamaṣṭaprakāro'ya jñānamālokya paścimam 
paścimājñāviśuddhā ye ślokārthapratipādakāḥ 
te  jānanti idaṃ śambho vimalaṃ pārameśvaram 
jñānamaṣṭaprakārasya śrīmataṃ saptakoṭikam 
devatānāṃ mukhāmnāyaṃ gūḍhārthamupadeśakam 
mahat kaṣṭataraṃ durgaṃ rudrāṃśo vetti paścimam 
na cāpi vindate martaya saṃpradāyamahauṣadham kumārikākhaṇḍa
kriyākārakasaṃbandhaṃ vibhaktilaghupratyayam' 
samāsaiḥ saptakairbheda guptaṃ kulavadhū iva 
kliṣṭaśabdairvibhajyeta tasmāt kliṣṭa tyajed budhaḥ 
apaśabdaiśca saralaistaistu śaivo'bhigamyate 
saṃketavarṇamekena mukhāmnāyena śodhayet 
na cāpi laṭaloṭaistu śuṣkatarkādibhistathā 
vyākhyāyāmāgame deva divyā vāṇī svatantrasthā 
viparītamidaṃ jñātvā divyāmnāyaḥ pravartate 
evaṃ pāṇḍityamutsṛjya sarala kaulikāgamam 
śrotavyaṃ ca mukhāmnāya karṇāt karṇāntarāgatam 
akṣarārthopadeśaśca saṃpradāyaśca kaulikaḥ 
nigarbhaśca ṣaḍevaite saṃpradāyā udāhṛtāḥ 
sāraṃ ślokopadeśa ca nirṇīta tava bhairava 
kaulikājñāparaṃ nāsti śrīmatāt parataraṃ na hi 
mukhāmnāyāt paraṃ nāsti śeṣaṃ tyajyaṃ palālavat 
evaṃ sañcintya yatnena mukhakaulaṃ samabhyaset 
ājñāvartiḥ śivaḥ panthā vṛkṣacchāyā somo raviḥ 
paraṃ paramahaṃsa ca kuvera pīṭhamāvalī 
kumārī kartarī bhāṣā mātrātmā mātarī tathā 
pūrvapaścimamadhya ca vāmadakṣiṇakoṇakam 
yoniṣaṭka ca śṛṅgā ādikṣānta kuleśvaram 
yo hi vetti idaṃ jñāna sa sākṣād bhairavaḥ svayaṃ 
kumārikākhaṇḍaḥ
evaṃ  kramārthatastattvaṃ saptakoṭyād vinirgatam 
yo hanet paśubhāvātmā  gurustena hanīkṛta 
paratraṃ hāritaṃ tena meru  tenaiva laṅgitam 
idaṃ matamidaṃ yogamidaṃ tattva kulārṇavam 
kulaugha kramaogha tu jñānaughaṃ ca tathottamam 
pūjanīyaṃ prayatnena hanyate na kadācana 
pañcasrotātmake śaive ṣaṣṭhe kulaviniścaye 
ajavaktrāt paraṃ śāntamidaṃ tat sārasaṃgraham 
siddhasantānasubhagaṃ pratyayājñāviśāradam 
nāmnā kramodayajñāna śrīkhageśīmahāmatam 
śrīnātha uvāca
satyametat tvayā proktaṃ kaulikaṃ pratyayātmakam 
kaulajñānāt paraṃ nāsti durlabhaṃ matasaṃgraham 
koṭikoṭirasaṃkhyātā mayā śāstrāvatāritāḥ 
pṛcchakānumatenaiva sarve te ca palālavat 
vibhāgaṃ ca pramāṇaṃ ca śāstramañjūṣakaṃ śṛṇu 
saptakoṭipramāṇena mataṃ vai pārameśvaram 
koṭipañcāśallakṣaika sahasraṃ śatasaṃkhyayā 
śatā  śatapādaṃ ca sadyojātād vinirgatam 
navanavatirlakṣāṇi lakṣakoṭistathaiva ca 
a
tathānyā koṭipañcāśad vāmadevād viniḥ śritāḥ
kumārikākhaṇḍa
koṭīnyayutacatvāri lakṣāḥ pañcāśakoṭikāḥ 
sahasraśatasaṃkhyā ca sahasraka śataṃ tathā 
śatalakṣasahasraṃ ca aghorāt tu vinirgatam 
arbudaṃ cārbuda caiva kharvaścaiva parāparam 
ṣaṭsahasrāṇi koṭiśca lakṣapādaṃ sahasrakam 
śatama ca pādākhyaṃ tatpuruṣācca vinirgatam 
īśānasya tu vaktrasya pañcamasya mahātmanaḥ 
vicāryato'pi yatnena śāstrasaṃkhyā na vidyate 
evaṃ vai śāstrāmnāyaṃ tu mataṃ jñātvā samabhyaset 
pañcaśrotodbhavā hyete granthasaṃkhyāsamanvitāḥ 
lokācārasya hetvarthe mayā te parikīrtitāḥ 
ṣaṣṭhamaṃ yanmahāvaktraṃ tad guptaṃ tu mayā kṛtam 
granthānāṃ tu śataṃ sārdhaṃ tasmād vaktrād vinirgatam 
sthitaṃ tat khecarīcakre nigūḍhe saṃprakāśitam  
śāstrāvatāramañjūṣaṃ kiñcid vakṣyāmyahaṃ śṛṇu
